### [79] [EntmaxKV: Support-Aware Decoding for Entmax Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21649)
*Gonçalo Duarte,Miguel Couceiro,Marcos V. Treviso*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: EntmaxKV通过引入具有精确稀疏特性的$α$-entmax注意力，在长文本解码中实现了一种高效、可控且精确的稀疏化策略，在大幅降低KV缓存读取开销的同时，保持了接近全注意力的推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长上下文解码受到KV缓存内存带宽的极大限制。现有的稀疏解码方法多基于softmax注意力，由于softmax总是产生非零概率，导致稀疏化本质上是不可控的近似；而$α$-entmax能够产生精确的零值，使得稀疏解码转化为支持集恢复问题，从而在计算效率和精确度之间取得更好的平衡。

Method: 提出了一种名为EntmaxKV的框架，利用$α$-entmax算子产生的稀疏性（精确零值）。该方法包含三个核心组件：1. 基于查询的页面评分机制；2. 支持集感知的候选挑选策略；3. 稀疏entmax注意力算子。此外，引入了高斯感知选择器，通过轻量级页面统计信息动态估计entmax阈值，从而自适应地调整计算预算。

Result: 实验表明，在长上下文和语言建模基准测试中，EntmaxKV在同等KV预算下，相比基于softmax的稀疏方法损失了更少的概率质量，保留了更多的支持集token，且输出误差更低。在1M上下文长度下，相比全注意力基准，实现了最高3.36倍（softmax基准）和5.43倍（entmax基准）的加速。

Conclusion: EntmaxKV成功实现了稀疏解码与$α$-entmax注意力的原生结合，通过在KV缓存加载前识别稀疏性，在保持高精度的同时显著提升了长上下文解码速度，为高效长上下文推理提供了一种可行且高效的方案。

Abstract: Long-context decoding is increasingly limited by KV-cache memory traffic since each generated token attends over a cache whose size grows linearly with context length. Existing sparse decoding methods reduce this cost by selecting subsets of tokens or pages, but are designed for softmax attention, whose dense tails make any truncation discard nonzero probability mass. In contrast, $α$-entmax produces exact zeros, turning sparse decoding from dense-tail approximation into support recovery: if the selected candidates contain the entmax support, sparse decoding remains exact. While recent entmax kernels enable efficient training, they do not address the autoregressive decoding bottleneck, where dense inference still streams the full KV cache before sparsity is known. In this work, we introduce EntmaxKV, an entmax-native sparse decoding framework that exploits sparsity before KV pages are loaded. EntmaxKV combines query-aware page scoring, support-aware candidate selection, and sparse entmax attention. We analyze truncation error through the dropped probability mass $δ$, showing that output error is controlled by $δ$ and vanishes when the entmax support is recovered. We further introduce a Gaussian-aware entmax selector that estimates the entmax threshold from lightweight page statistics, adapting the selected budget to the score distribution. Empirically, EntmaxKV drops less probability mass, retains more support tokens, and achieves lower output error than softmax-based sparse decoding at matched KV budgets. On long-context and language modeling benchmarks, it closely matches full-cache entmax while using a small fraction of the KV cache, achieving up to $3.36\times$ (softmax) and $5.43\times$ (entmax) speedup over full attention baselines at 1M context length. Code available at: https://github.com/deep-spin/entmaxkv.

</details>


### [80] [Amplifying, Not Learning: Fine-Tuned AI Text Detectors Amplify a Pretrained Direction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21653)
*Alexander Smirnov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: AI文本检测器并非真的在区分AI与人，而是在识别预训练模型中的“典型性”特征。研究通过实证分析表明，简单的向量投影或小样本探针已能达到目前微调模型的水平，且现有的检测器在面对非母语写作时存在严重的逻辑偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在挑战当前AI文本检测器的工作原理假设，即它们并非在构建真实的AI与人类界限，而是放大了预训练模型中的典型性轴线。研究者试图揭示检测器在不同架构、不同样本群体下的内在机制及局限性。

Method: 研究采用了多种分析手段：1. 直接在未经微调的原始编码器上进行向量投影分析；2. 使用少样本（24个示例）冻结探针进行评估；3. 引入闭式雅可比预测器（Closed-form Jacobian predictor）来量化和干预模型轴向；4. 通过三种操作上独立的探针（大小写比率残差化、几何有符号ε消融、文本对预测器）验证观测的一致性。

Result: 研究发现，原始编码器直接投影即可达到微调模型近乎一致的性能（甚至在RoBERTa-base上超过微调）；在非母语（ESL）文本中，检测轴线甚至会发生反转；利用闭式雅可比预测器可以极大地提升现有检测器的性能，并证实了大部分微调带来的提升实际上是校准偏移。

Conclusion: AI文本检测器本质上是基于“典型性（typicality）”而非真正的“AI与人类”分类边界。目前的检测方法主要是在预训练模型的特征空间中识别AI生成的文本模式，这种方法在非母语写作中容易失效，且许多所谓的“微调”提升仅仅是校准偏移而非学习到了更深层的语义表征。

Abstract: AI text detectors amplify a pretrained typicality axis; they do not construct an AI-vs-human boundary. On raw encoders before any task supervision, projecting onto centroid(AI)-centroid(HC3) achieves NYT-vs-HC3 AUROC 0.806/0.944/0.834 across three architectures (86-106% of the fine-tuned discrimination ceiling: on RoBERTa-base, raw projection exceeds fine-tuning); on RoBERTa-base, full fine-tuning reduces discrimination below raw on both fluent-formal populations tested. The same axis inverts on non-native ESL writing (AUROC 0.06-0.20) -- a falsifiable prediction unique to the typicality reading. A 24-example frozen probe matches full fine-tuning (0.900 vs 0.895). A closed-form Jacobian predictor parameterises axis-manipulating interventions with R^2 = 1.000 universal, lifts ELECTRA-CE deployment TPR from 0.000 to 0.904 at FPR = 1%, and transfers to three independently-trained third-party RoBERTa detectors at 16/16 oracle-equivalence (57% NYT-FPR reduction on the OpenAI detector). Scope: encoder family; mechanism magnitude HC3-anchored; population-level shared axis with per-text mechanisms varying across architectures. Three operationally distinct probes -- text-surface caps_rate residualisation, geometric signed-epsilon ablation, closed-form text-pair predictor -- agree at cos 0.74/0.81/1.00 across three architectures, confirming observer-invariance. Under matched-TPR-0.90 evaluation, the published intervention zoo (CC, dealign-f2c) is calibration-equivalent across 27 cells (|Delta AUROC| <= 0.0081), and >= 97% of the LoRA->full-FT bias gap on ELECTRA is calibration shift, not learned representation -- the central claim's prediction confirmed.

</details>


### [81] [Value-Gradient Hypothesis of RL for LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21654)
*Arip Asadulaev,Daniil Ognev,Karim Salta,Martin Takac*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了无评论员（critic-free）强化学习（如PPO）在LLM训练中有效的深层机制：通过反向传播隐式构建价值梯度，并建立了衡量RL收益的理论框架，指导模型在何时引入RL最为高效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管PPO和GRPO等无评论员（critic-free）强化学习方法在大型语言模型（LLM）的后训练阶段表现优异，但其内在机理尚不明确，且缺乏关于在何种条件下RL能提供最大增益的理论指导。该论文旨在从理论上阐释这些算法为何有效，并界定其适用场景。

Method: 1. 提出价值梯度视角：通过可微分展开（differentiable rollout）和加性噪声参数化分析演员更新（actor update）。
2. 数学证明：证明在期望意义下，演员更新通过反向传播产生的伴随状态（costates）近似于价值梯度。
3. 针对离散变换器策略的分析：分析自微分（autodifferentiation）如何通过注意力机制产生近似价值信号的经验伴随状态，并论证误差与采样间隙及策略熵相关。
4. 归因分解：提出将RL的有效性分解为价值梯度信号与可达奖励空间（reward headroom）。

Result: 1. 理论上揭示了无评论员RL方法中的演员更新本质上是在进行价值梯度估计。
2. 证明了反向传播在离散Transformer策略中能够生成有效的“经验伴随状态”，从而实现价值信号的隐式学习。
3. 提出了基于价值梯度和奖励空间的分析框架，能够有效判断RL在预训练的不同阶段所能产生的预期收益。

Conclusion: 该研究通过价值梯度视角证明了无评论员（critic-free）强化学习算法（如PPO和GRPO）在语言模型微调中的有效性原理。研究确立了RL改进的分解框架，指出RL的增益效果取决于价值梯度信号的强度与可达奖励空间的余量，并为预测RL在预训练轨迹中的最佳应用时机提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning substantially improves pretrained language models, but it remains understudied why critic-free methods such as PPO and GRPO work as well as they do, and when they should provide the largest gains. We develop a value-gradient perspective of critic-free RL for LLM post-training. First, under a differentiable rollout and additive-noise parameterization, we show that the actor update is value-gradient-like in expectation: the backward pass propagates costates whose conditional expectation equals the value gradient. Second, for discrete transformer policies, we show that autodifferentiation through attention produces empirical costates that approximate this value signal, with an error controlled by the sampling gap and policy entropy. These results motivate a decomposition of RL impact into value gradient signal and reachable reward headroom, yielding a criterion for when RL should be most effective along a pretraining trajectory.

</details>


### [82] [Hierarchical Variational Policies for Reward-Guided Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21661)
*Kushagra Pandey,Farrin Marouf Sofian,Jan Niklas Groeneveld,Felix Draxler,Stephan Mandt*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对扩散模型的快速摊销采样框架，通过学习轻量级随机策略取代昂贵的测试时引导，大幅降低了推理成本，同时在图像质量和生成速度上均优于现有的测试时缩放基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的预训练扩散模型适配下游任务（如反问题）通常需要昂贵的测试时引导或复杂的优化过程，推理成本过高。本文旨在开发一种能在显著降低推理成本的前提下，生成高质量且符合特定奖励目标样本的通用框架。

Method: 提出了一种分层变分模型，将推理过程中的控制能力摊销至一个轻量级且具有表达能力的随机策略中。该方法支持少步扩散采样，利用大步长实现快速推理，并由学习到的策略进行每步结构化控制。此外，还引入了“半摊销”机制，即结合摊销建议与受限的测试时优化。

Result: 在多种具有挑战性的反问题（如4倍超分辨率）中，该方法实现了优异的质量与速度权衡，相比当前最佳基准，推理速度提升超过5倍，且感知质量更高。在半摊销模式下，该方法在多项任务中达到了最优的感知质量。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种将测试时适应转化为分层变分问题的框架，通过轻量级随机策略实现了扩散模型采样的完全摊销。该方法在保证高质量生成的同时，显著提升了推理速度，并可通过结合有限的测试时优化进一步达到最佳性能。

Abstract: Adapting pretrained diffusion models to downstream objectives such as inverse problems often requires expensive test-time guidance or optimization. We propose a principled framework for generating high-quality reward-aligned samples at substantially reduced inference cost. Our approach formulates test-time adaptation as a hierarchical variational model, where control is amortized into a lightweight yet expressive stochastic policy. This formulation naturally supports few-step diffusion sampling: large step sizes enable fast inference, while the learned policy maintains sample quality by providing structured per-step control. The resulting fully amortized sampler achieves a strong quality--speed tradeoff, matching or exceeding recent test-time scaling baselines while requiring significantly less compute. For example, on 4x super-resolution, our method achieves better perceptual quality with more than 5x faster inference compared to the best-performing baseline. We further extend our approach to a semi-amortized regime that combines cheap amortized proposals with limited test-time optimization, achieving state-of-the-art perceptual quality across several challenging inverse problems.

### [83] [I-SAFE: Wasserstein Coherence Metrics for Structural Auditing of Scientific AI Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21731)
*Barbara Tarantino,Gennaro Auricchio,Paolo Giudici*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 I-SAFE 框架，通过结构化输入扰动和 Wasserstein 一致性度量，对科学 AI 模型进行事后审计，从而识别出模型对科学规律的遵循程度及其隐藏的分布偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学领域的深度学习模型常被批评仅利用数据集的捷径特征（shortcuts）或偏差而非领域知识，导致其在高准确率下可能存在科学解释性缺失或泛化风险。研究旨在解决如何评估这些模型是否真正遵循了领域相关的结构规律。

Method: 提出了 I-SAFE（Interventional Secure, Accurate, Fair and Explainable）审计框架。该方法基于 Wasserstein 一致性度量（WCM），结合外部领域知识结构先验，对预训练的黑盒模型进行输入层面的结构化扰动，并从位置、序数和形状三个维度量化输出分布的一致性。

Result: 在药物-靶点相互作用（DTI）预测任务中，I-SAFE 成功揭示了尽管 DeepConvDTI、DeepDTA 和 TAPB 三个模型具有相似的预测准确率，但它们对输入结构扰动的反应分布存在显著差异，表明单一的准确率指标不足以衡量模型的科学可靠性。

Conclusion: I-SAFE 框架通过引入 Wasserstein 一致性度量（WCM）和结构化扰动，为评估科学 AI 模型在处理分布外数据时的可靠性提供了一种与模型无关、事后审计的有效途径，能够揭示传统准确率指标无法捕捉的深层偏差。

Abstract: Deep learning models are increasingly used in scientific prediction tasks where strong benchmark performance is often interpreted as evidence of scientifically meaningful behavior. This interpretation is fragile, as models may exploit shortcut features, dataset-specific regularities, or distributional biases that are predictive on held-out data but not aligned with domain-relevant structure. To address this limitation, we introduce the \textsc{I-SAFE} (Interventional Secure, Accurate, Fair and Explainable) framework, a post-hoc distributional auditing framework for scientific AI models centered on the Wasserstein Coherence Metric (WCM). Given a trained black-box predictor and an external structural prior encoding domain knowledge about task-relevant input structure, \textsc{I-SAFE} evaluates raw model outputs under structurally guided perturbations of the input. The proposed audit measures output-distribution coherence through three complementary metrics: a Quantile-Based Metric (QBM) for location-level coherence, the WCM for ordinal coherence, and a translation-invariant WCM variant for shape coherence. We instantiate \textsc{I-SAFE} on drug--target interaction (DTI) prediction using the Davis kinase benchmark, KLIFS (Kinase--Ligand Interaction Fingerprints and Structures) binding-pocket annotations, and three sequence-based DTI models: DeepConvDTI, DeepDTA, and TAPB. Although the models operate in a comparable predictive regime, \textsc{I-SAFE} reveals substantially different distributional response profiles, a distinction invisible to accuracy-based evaluation. The framework is model-agnostic and applicable to any domain where inputs admit a structured decomposition and an external prior is available.

### [84] [Quantitative coronary calcification analysis for prediction of myocardial ischemia using non-contrast CT calcium scoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21745)
*Juhwan Lee,Sadeer Al-Kindi,Ammar Hoori,Tao Hu,Hao Wu,Justin N. Kim,Robert Gilkeson,Sanjay Rajagopalan,David L. Wilson*

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一种基于非增强CT钙化扫描的机器学习框架，通过引入深度钙质组学特征，实现了对心肌缺血的高效预测，显著优于传统风险评估手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非增强CTCS是评估心血管风险的常用工具，但其主要指标（如Agatston评分）在预测心肌缺血方面的灵敏度有限。研究旨在开发一种利用常规CTCS扫描数据的新型机器学习框架，通过提取更深层的钙化特征（钙质组学）来提高对心肌缺血的预测准确性。

Method: 研究人员对1,375名同时接受非增强CTCS和心脏PET心肌灌注成像的患者进行了回顾性分析。利用XGBoost算法结合SHAP解释方法从74个临床及钙化特征变量中进行特征筛选，构建了包含Agatston评分、8个钙质组学特征及年龄的机器学习预测模型，并采用5折交叉验证评估模型性能。

Result: 模型在987名患者的数据集中表现出色，精确率为98.9%，灵敏度为79.2%，F1评分为87.7%。对比实验表明，加入钙质组学特征后的模型性能显著优于仅使用临床变量或临床变量加Agatston评分的模型（p<0.05）。此外，逻辑回归分析显示，受累钙化动脉数量与心肌缺血存在最强关联。

Conclusion: 通过引入“钙质组学”（calcium-omics）特征，基于常规非增强CTCS扫描的机器学习模型能够显著提升对心肌缺血的预测能力。该方法为心血管风险分层提供了一种无创、低成本且高效的新策略，可作为临床决策的辅助工具。

Abstract: Non-contrast computed tomography calcium scoring (CTCS) is widely recognized as an effective tool for cardiovascular risk stratification. This study aimed to develop a novel machine learning framework for predicting myocardial ischemia from routine non-contrast CTCS scans using quantitative coronary calcium assessment. This study analyzed 1,375 patients who underwent both non-contrast CTCS and regadenoson stress cardiac positron emission tomography myocardial perfusion imaging within one year at University Hospitals Cleveland Medical Center. A total of 74 variables, including clinical variables, Agatston score, and calcium-omics features, were evaluated. Relevant features were identified using XGBoost with Shapley Additive exPlanations (SHAP). Predictive models were trained and evaluated using 5-fold cross-validation. Among 987 patients, 89 (9%) were positive for myocardial ischemia. The final model incorporated the Agatston score, eight calcium-omics features, and age. The proposed model achieved a precision of 98.9+/-3.0%, sensitivity of 79.2+/-8.4, and F1 score of 87.7+/-5.3%. The addition of calcium-omics features significantly improved predictive performance compared with models using clinical variables alone or clinical variables with the Agatston score (p<0.05). Interestingly, the number of calcified arteries, despite being the lowest-ranked feature based on SHAP analysis, showed the strongest association with myocardial ischemia in logistic regression analysis (odds ratio: 3.63, 95% confidence interval: 2.80-4.77, p<0.00001). We developed a machine learning approach for predicting myocardial ischemia using routinely acquired non-contrast CTCS scans. Calcium-omics features provided incremental predictive value beyond conventional risk factors and Agatston scoring and may support more accessible cardiovascular risk stratification.

### [85] [Models Can Model, But Can't Bind: Structured Grounding in Text-to-Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21751)
*Zhiqi Gao,Albert Ge,Alexander Berenbeim,Nathaniel D. Bastian,Frederic Sala*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大模型在求解优化问题时因参数绑定误差导致的精度衰减问题，本文提出了BIND方法，通过将数据绑定流程外化为编程操作，在降低计算成本的同时显著提升了求解准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前的大模型在处理“文本到优化”（Text-to-optimization）任务时，随着实例数据规模增大，性能会出现“有效绑定极限”（effective binding limit）导致精度剧降。作者旨在解决模型在处理复杂参数绑定时的准确性瓶颈，并区分建模与绑定这两项核心能力。

Method: 1. 提出了Text2Opt-Bench基准测试，涵盖12种优化问题分类；2. 提出了BIND（Binding-Inference-Normalization-Data）方法：通过将数值数据外化为结构化文件，使模型能够通过编程方式绑定数据，而非直接从提示词中转录；3. 通过专门针对数据绑定能力的微调（Finetuning）验证了该能力的独立价值。

Result: 1. 发现随着问题实例数据量增加，模型准确率会出现显著下降，即存在“有效绑定极限”；2. 使用BIND方法后，GPT-5-Nano的准确率从59.1%提升至82.4%，GPT-5从86.2%提升至95.8%；3. 专精于绑定能力的1.5B参数模型性能可匹配7B参数的端到端基线模型，证明了专注绑定任务的有效性。

Conclusion: 研究证明，将模型的数据绑定能力与建模能力分离是提升大模型求解优化问题的关键。通过引入BIND方法，模型能够更可靠地处理大规模数据，从而在无需大规模参数扩展的情况下显著提升求解精度。

Abstract: Text-to-optimization requires two separable capabilities: modeling -- choosing the right optimization structure -- and binding -- grounding every coefficient, index, and parameter in the concrete problem data. We study this via Text2Opt-Bench, a scalable benchmark of solver-verified optimization problems spanning 12 categories, from textbook linear programs to stochastic and multi-objective formulations with up to thousands of variables. Across 10+ models, we find that accuracy collapses as instance data grows, even when the formulation itself is simple. We call this the effective binding limit. We address this via a simple inference-time approach, BIND, which externalizes numeric data to structured files so the model binds data programmatically rather than transcribing from the prompt. BIND improves GPT-5-Nano from 59.1% to 82.4% accuracy, matching pass@5 (82.0%) at lower token cost than pass@1, and GPT-5 from 86.2% to 95.8%. Furthermore, we validate our hypothesis by finetuning a model exclusively on binding and show that it outperforms end-to-end SFT and RL across three structurally distinct optimization categories, with a 1.5B binding specialist alone matching a 7B end-to-end baseline.

### [86] [PEARL: Unbiased Percentile Estimation via Contrastive Learning for Industrial-Scale Livestream Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21752)
*Blake Gella,Wei Wu,Yuhao Yin,Zexi Huang,Zikai Wang,Emily Liu,Junlin Zhang,Wentao Guo,Qinglei Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对推荐系统中用户活跃度不均导致的偏差，本文提出了 PEARL 框架，通过对比式百分位近似技术消除行为强度偏见，在工业级大规模应用中取得了显著的推荐质量提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推荐系统中的行为强度失衡（即不同活跃度用户间的交互模式差异）会导致反馈信号失真，模型过度依赖活跃用户，从而降低推荐的质量与鲁棒性。

Method: 提出了一种非参数化的对比百分位近似框架 PEARL。该方法利用真实的对比交互样本直接近似百分位关系，无需辅助分布估计；引入了基于预测的自助法（bootstrapping）进行百分位平滑以处理稀疏数据，并结合广义价值加权及协同训练策略来增强模型表示能力。

Result: 离线实验表明 PEARL 能有效缓解行为偏差并提升排名性能；在拥有数十亿用户的直播平台线上 A/B 测试中，观看时长提升 2.10%，消费金额提升 0.80%，互动率提升 1.49%，举报率降低 6.91%。

Conclusion: PEARL 框架通过建模相对偏好而非绝对互动强度，有效解决了推荐系统中的行为强度失衡问题，并在离线实验与大规模线上生产环境中均表现出显著的性能提升。

Abstract: Recommender systems trained on user interaction data are susceptible to behavioral intensity imbalance--a systematic distortion arising from heterogeneous engagement patterns across users. This imbalance skews feedback signals such that observed interactions no longer faithfully reflect true preferences, causing models to disproportionately amplify signals from highly active users while underrepresenting others, which ultimately degrades recommendation quality and robustness at scale. To address this issue, we propose a nonparametric contrastive percentile approximation framework, PEARL, that models relative preference signals instead of absolute engagement magnitudes. Building upon relative advantage debiasing, PEARL leverages real contrastive interaction samples to approximate percentile relationships directly, without relying on auxiliary distribution estimation models. We provide theoretical justification demonstrating that such pairwise comparisons yield unbiased estimates of percentile-based preference signals. For broader applicability, we introduce a prediction-based bootstrapping mechanism for percentile smoothing to handle sparse and discrete feedback, alongside a generalized value-weighted formulation and a co-training strategy to enhance both modeling flexibility and representation learning. Extensive offline experiments demonstrate that PEARL effectively mitigates behavioral bias and consistently improves recommendation performance across multiple ranking targets. Deployed in a production livestream platform with a combined user base of billions, online A/B testing confirms substantial real-world gains: +2.10% Watch Duration, +0.80% Consumption Amount, +1.49% Interaction Rate, and -6.91% Report Rate.

Abstract: Non-contrast computed tomography calcium scoring (CTCS) is a cost-effective imaging modality widely used to detect coronary artery calcifications. Predictive modeling utilized the CatBoost gradient boosting method, focusing on the most informative features. From an initial set of 424 candidate features, 14 were identified as most predictive through the CatBoost-SHAP method. The top two predictive features originated from fat-omics, with the remaining 12 features derived from calcium-omics. The optimized model achieved robust predictive capabilities, demonstrating a sensitivity of 83.1+/-4.6%, specificity of 93.8+/-1.7%, accuracy of 85.3+/-2.0%, and an F1 score of 73.9+/-3.3%. Notably, the model also showed reliable predictive accuracy in patients with diverse coronary calcium scores, including cases with obstructive CAD despite a zero-calcium score. This innovative approach holds promise for improving clinical decision-making and potentially reducing dependence on contrast-enhanced or invasive diagnostic procedures, particularly within low-to intermediate-risk patient groups.

### [88] [On the Sample Complexity of Discounted Reinforcement Learning with Optimized Certainty Equivalents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21763)
*Oliver Mortensen,Mohammad Sadegh Talebi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了基于生成模型的风险敏感强化学习，明确了OCE框架下PAC可学习性的充要条件，证明了当效用函数定义域受限时问题不可学习，并优化了CVaR风险度量下的样本复杂度界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究采用基于模型（model-based）的方法进行学习，通过优化确定性等价（OCE）框架定义目标函数，利用PAC（概率近似正确）学习理论推导样本复杂度上界，并构建相应的下界以验证理论的紧致性。

Result: 证明了当效用函数定义域非全域（dom(u)≠R）时，问题不可PAC学习；推导了OCE目标下的PAC样本复杂度上界；对于CVaR_τ，将样本复杂度对τ的依赖提升至1/τ²，且证明了所提出的下界在状态-动作空间大小SA上的依赖是紧致的。

Conclusion: 该研究明确了风险敏感强化学习在PAC可学习性方面的边界，证明了效用函数的定义域是决定问题能否被有效学习的关键因素，并为CVaR等特定风险度量提供了改进的样本复杂度界限。

Abstract: We study risk-sensitive reinforcement learning in finite discounted MDPs, where a generative model of the MDP is assumed to be available. We consider a family or risk measures called the optimized certainty equivalent (OCE), which includes important risk measures such as entropic risk, CVaR, and mean-variance. Our focus is on the sample complexities of learning the optimal state-action value function (value learning) and an optimal policy (policy learning) under recursive OCE. We provide an exact characterization of utility functions $u$ for which the corresponding OCE defines an objective that is PAC-learnable. We analyze a simple model-based approach and derive PAC sample complexity bounds. We establish that whenever $u$ does not have full domain $\text{dom}(u)\neq \mathbb{R}$, the corresponding problem is not PAC-learnable. Finally, we establish corresponding lower bounds for both value and policy learning, demonstrating tightness in the size $SA$ of state-action space, and for a more restricted class of utilities, we derive lower bounds that makes the dependence on the effective horizon $\frac{1}{1-γ}$ explicit. Specifically, for $\text{CVaR}_τ$ we show that the correct dependence on $τ$ is $\frac{1}{τ^2}$, thus improving by a factor of $\frac{1}τ$ over state-of-the-art although our bound has a suboptimal dependence on $\frac{1}{1-γ}$.

### [89] [Provable Robustness against Backdoor Attacks via the Primal-Dual Perspective on Differential Privacy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21780)
*Aman Saxena,Jan Schuchardt,Yan Scholten,Stephan Günnemann*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于隐私概况的通用框架，首次实现了对后门攻击中训练时和推理时联合随机机制的端到端健壮性认证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的随机平滑技术主要针对训练时（投毒）或推理时（规避）的单一攻击场景。针对同时存在训练和测试数据扰动的后门攻击，缺乏有效的统一健壮性认证框架，难以将训练时和推理时的随机化机制整合在同一个分析体系中。

Method: 提出了一个基于“隐私概况（Privacy Profiles）”的框架，将随机平滑与差分隐私的对偶视角连接起来。该方法利用隐私概况提供了一种组合异构机制的数值化程序，从而能够模块化地计算联合认证边界，并应用于 DP-SGD（差分隐私随机梯度下降）和深度分区聚合（Deep Partition Aggregation）等机制。

Result: 实验结果表明，该框架在 MNIST 和 CIFAR-10 数据集上能有效对组合机制进行认证。它成功为 DP-SGD 和深度分区聚合机制推导出了针对训练时和推理时攻击的联合健壮性保证，展示了该方法在处理复杂现实威胁模型下的有效性和通用性。

Conclusion: 该论文通过隐私概况将随机平滑与差分隐私的对偶视角相结合，为评估和防御复杂的后门攻击提供了一个通用且严谨的端到端认证框架，有效弥补了现有随机化机制在联合训练和推理攻击防御方面的不足。

Abstract: Randomized smoothing is a powerful tool for certifying robustness to adversarial perturbations, including poisoning attacks via randomized training and evasion attacks via randomized inference. Extending these guarantees to backdoor attacks, where training and test data are jointly perturbed, remains challenging because training- and test-time randomized mechanisms must be analyzed within a single robustness certificate. We address this by connecting randomized smoothing to the dual view of differential privacy through privacy profiles, which provide a numerical procedure for composing heterogeneous mechanisms. The resulting framework enables tight, modular, end-to-end certification of complex, composed mechanisms while leveraging existing analyses of differentially private mechanisms. We instantiate the framework for DP-SGD and Deep Partition Aggregation with inference-time smoothing, deriving joint robustness guarantees against both training-time and inference-time attacks. Experiments on MNIST and CIFAR-10 demonstrate the effectiveness of our framework. Overall, we provide a principled and general framework for using composite mechanisms to certify robustness under complex threat models that better capture the capabilities of real-world adversaries.

### [90] [MMD-Balls as Credal Sets: A PAC-Bayesian Framework for Epistemic Uncertainty in Test-Time Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21783)
*Ahanaf Hasan Ariq*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个基于PAC-Bayesian理论和不精确概率论的框架，通过MMD量化测试时适应（TTA）中的分布偏移，从而提供可靠的泛化误差界及认知不确定性度量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的测试时适应（TTA）方法虽能提升分布偏移下的模型性能，但缺乏描述偏移幅度与预测可靠性之间关系的理论保证，且难以有效地量化认知不确定性。

Method: 1. 构建了基于PAC-Bayesian框架的泛化界，显式地以源分布与目标分布之间的最大均值差异（MMD）为参数；2. 利用Walley的不精确概率理论，将源分布周边的MMD球解释为认知集；3. 在RKHS-Lipschitz损失假设下推导了偏移惩罚界；4. 利用MMD集中不等式推导出有限样本版本；5. 分析了测地线保持（geodesic preservation）边界，揭示了核引导适应对局部特征几何的保护机制。

Result: 提出了一个包含MMD依赖项的PAC-Bayesian泛化界，实现了对分布偏移下风险的量化；证明了在认知集内对所有分布的均匀最差情况风险界，并给出了上下风险分解；阐明了核引导适应在保持局部特征几何结构方面的理论优越性。

Conclusion: 通过将MMD球解释为认知集（Credal sets），该研究成功地将PAC-Bayesian学习理论与不精确概率理论结合，为测试时适应（TTA）提供了一种严谨的数学框架，有效分离了认知不确定性和偶然不确定性，并为何时进行模型适应提供了原则性的决策依据。

Abstract: Test-time adaptation (TTA) methods improve model performance under distribution shift but lack formal guarantees connecting shift magnitude to prediction reliability. We develop a PAC-Bayesian framework yielding generalization bounds explicitly parameterized by the maximum mean discrepancy (MMD) between source and target distributions. Our principal contribution is interpreting MMD-balls around the source distribution as credal sets in Walley's imprecise probability theory, yielding natural epistemic uncertainty quantification. We establish: (i) a PAC-Bayesian bound with an MMD-dependent shift penalty under an RKHS-Lipschitz loss assumption; (ii) a finite-sample version via MMD concentration; (iii) a uniform worst-case risk bound over all distributions in the credal set, with a lower-upper risk decomposition; and (iv) geodesic preservation bounds explaining why kernel-guided adaptation protects local feature geometry. The credal set interpretation separates epistemic from aleatoric uncertainty and provides a principled decision criterion for when adaptation is warranted.

Abstract: World models are central to building agents that can reason, plan, and generalize beyond their training data. Current practice is further limited by three key bottlenecks: fragile one-off codebases, slow video data loading, and the lack of standardized generalization benchmarks. We present stable-worldmodel (swm), an open-source platform for standardized and reproducible world modeling research and evaluation. It delivers (1) a high-performance Lance-based data layer with native support and conversion tools for MP4, HDF5, and LeRobot datasets, (2) clean, well-tested implementations of modern world model baselines and planning solvers, and (3) a broad suite of environments and tasks extended with controllable visual, geometric, and physical factors of variation for systematic in-silico evaluation of dynamics understanding, control performance, representation quality, and out-of-distribution generalization. ### [92] [Why Semantic Entropy Fails: Geometry-Aware and Calibrated Uncertainty for Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21801)
*Zheyuan Zhang,Kaiwen Shi,Han Bao,Zehong Wang,Tianyi Ma,Yanfang Ye*

Method: 1. 理论分析：识别了现有基于熵的估计器存在的“各向异性间隙”（Anisotropic gap）和“校准间隙”（Calibration gap）。
2. 提出 GCPO 框架：引入几何感知（Geometry-aware）度量来捕捉语义分歧，并结合基于奖励的校准机制，使不确定性信号与学习信号强度相匹配。

Result: 实验表明，GCPO 能更准确地跟踪梯度变异性，并在多个基准测试中持续提升了模型后训练的性能。

Conclusion: GCPO 通过将不确定性信号与优化动力学相结合，为模型训练提供了一个原则性的框架。研究表明，设计与梯度变异性对齐的不确定性度量对于提升强化学习训练的稳定性及模型推理能力至关重要。

Abstract: Post-training has become central to improving reasoning and alignment in large language models, where critic-free models enable scalable learning from model-generated outputs but lack principled mechanisms to distinguish informative from noisy signals. Recent approaches leverage response-level measures as uncertainty signals to regulate group-based optimization methods such as GRPO. Yet their empirical success remains unstable and unclear in how they influence optimization dynamics. In this paper, we provide, to our knowledge, the first principled formulation that interprets uncertainty signals as mechanisms for characterizing and regulating gradient variance and learning signal quality. Based on both empirical and theoretical analysis, we identify two critical gaps of current entropy-based estimators: The anisotropic gap and The calibration gap. Motivated by this analysis, we propose Geometric-aware Calibrated Policy Optimization (GCPO), a novel framework integrating geometry-aware measures to capture semantic disagreement with reward-based calibration to align uncertainty with learning signal strength. Experiments on multiple benchmarks show that our approach more faithfully tracks gradient variability and consistently improves post-training performance. Our results highlight the importance of designing uncertainty signals that are aligned with optimization dynamics, offering a principled perspective for robust post-training.

### [95] [On-Policy Consistency Training Improves LLM Safety with Minimal Capability Degradation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21834)

Existing consistency training procedures generate the supervision signal once, offline, and use supervised fine-tuning (SFT) to update the model. Unfortunately, the resulting models tend to merely memorize the surface forms of the training distribution and thus generalize poorly and regress in their capabilities. We evaluate OPCT on three safety axes: sycophancy, jailbreaking, and safety awareness. Across three model families, OPCT outperforms its SFT counterpart on all safety desiderata. Under an adaptive per-target attacker, OPCT holds jailbreak defense success near 99% on held-out jailbreak behaviors, whereas SFT achieves 87% on average. On safety awareness, OPCT outperforms SFT in two out of three models, and matches it on the other. OPCT also largely avoids the capability regressions that SFT induces, such as a 28-point drop on MATH-500. Our results suggest that consistency training is best implemented as OPCT rather than as SFT, especially when generalization beyond the training distribution is desired.

### [96] [Energy-Gated Attention: Spectral Salience as an Inductive Bias for Transformer Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21842)
*Athanasios Zeris*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种“能量门控注意力（EGA）”机制，通过识别并聚焦高频谱能量的“信息密集型”词元，在几乎不增加额外开销的情况下，有效提升了Transformer模型在多项语言任务上的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Transformer注意力机制对所有词元一视同仁，忽略了词元间存在的信息密度差异。受流体动力学中“相干结构”概念的启发，作者认为语言中也存在类似的关键信息载体，应根据词元的频谱能量赋予其不同的注意力权重，以提高模型处理效率和表现。

Method: 提出了一种名为能量门控注意力（Energy-Gated Attention, EGA）的改进方法。该方法在执行常规的注意力值聚合之前，通过一个轻量级的线性投影计算键（Key）嵌入的频谱能量，并利用该能量对注意力聚合进行门控，从而实现对信息密集型词元的加权增强。该方法几乎不增加计算开销。

Result: 在TinyShakespeare和Penn Treebank数据集上，EGA在几乎不增加参数量（<0.26%）和计算成本的前提下，显著降低了验证集损失（分别提升0.103和0.101）。实验还发现，学习到的能量阈值（τ≈0.35）与英语中内容词的比例高度吻合，且最优投影方式是数据自适应的。

Conclusion: 能量门控注意力（EGA）机制证明了在Transformer注意力计算中引入基于频谱能量的门控是有效的。研究表明，并非所有词元（token）的重要性均等，识别并增强信息密集型词元（如内容词）可以显著提升模型性能，且该机制具有良好的数据集普适性。此外，最优能量投影是数据驱动的，而非预定义的固定基函数。

Abstract: Standard transformer attention computes pairwise similarity between queries and keys, treating all tokens as equally salient regardless of their intrinsic informational content. In turbulent fluid dynamics, coherent structures -- the energetically dominant, spatially organized patterns that persist amid background chaos -- carry a disproportionate fraction of total energy and govern all transport. We propose that tokens play an analogous role in transformer attention: informationally dense positions (morphological boundaries, syntactic heads, discourse markers) concentrate spectral energy and should attract proportionally more attention than background tokens (function words, repeated patterns, low-information filler). We propose Energy-Gated Attention (EGA): a simple modification that gates value aggregation by the spectral energy of key token embeddings, computed by a single learned linear projection that discovers the dominant spectral mode of the embedding field. On TinyShakespeare, EGA achieves +0.103 validation loss improvement with only 12,480 additional parameters (<0.26% overhead) and no measurable computational cost. The result is consistent on Penn Treebank (+0.101), demonstrating dataset independence. A systematic ablation across three wavelet families (fixed Morlet, Daubechies db2/db4, and a parametric Morlet) establishes that fixed structured bases are suboptimal -- the optimal energy direction is data-adaptive and non-sinusoidal -- while identifying learned wavelet packets as a promising open direction. The learned energy threshold converges to tau ~= 0.35 independently of initialization, corresponding to the fraction (~36%) of tokens carrying above-average spectral energy in English text, a stable linguistic property consistent with the fraction of content words in running English text.

### [97] [Geometry-Adaptive Explainer for Faithful Dictionary-Based Interpretability under Distribution Shift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21849)
*Sungjun Lim,Heedong Kim,Andrew Lee,Kyungwoo Song*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究发现字典类解释器（如稀疏自编码器）在面对分布外（OOD）偏移时，其捕捉到的特征与模型实际使用的激活子空间会发生错位（即“忠实度差距”），导致解释性能严重下降。

Method: 提出了几何适应性解释器（GAE），该方法通过利用未标记的OOD激活数据，动态调整解释器字典以与OOD活跃子空间对齐，无需进行任何梯度更新或重新训练。

Result: 实验表明，GAE在多个模型和OOD设置下的因果忠实度指标上，表现优于未经调整的解释器，甚至达到或超过了现有的基于训练的基准方法。此外，理论分析证明其过量损失受二阶矩偏移的二次方约束。

Conclusion: 通过几何适应性解释器（GAE），无需梯度更新即可在分布外（OOD）数据上有效重构模型激活，从而在不损害原有特征结构的前提下，显著提升了机械解释工具在分布偏移下的忠实度。

Abstract: Mechanistic interpretability aims to explain a model's behavior by identifying causally responsible internal structures. Dictionary-based explainers such as sparse autoencoders and transcoders are a primary tool, but their faithfulness under out-of-distribution (OOD) shift has received little systematic attention. We show that distribution shift rotates the subspace that the model actively uses, misaligning the explainer's dictionary trained on in-distribution (ID) activations. We formalize this misalignment as the faithfulness gap, a geometric distance between the ID dictionary and the OOD-active subspace, and show that it controls OOD faithfulness degradation. To reduce this gap, we propose the Geometry-Adaptive Explainer (GAE), which realigns the explainer's dictionary with the OOD-active subspace while preserving the original feature structure. This requires only unlabeled OOD activations and no gradient updates. We prove that GAE improves over the unadapted ID explainer, with excess loss bounded quadratically by the second-moment shift. Empirically, GAE even matches or surpasses all training-based baselines in causal faithfulness across multiple models and OOD settings.

### [98] [The Illusion of Reasoning: Exposing Evasive Data Contamination in LLMs via Zero-CoT Truncation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21856)
*Yifan Lan,Yuanpu Cao,Hanyu Wang,Lu Lin,Jinghui Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Zero-CoT Probe (ZCP)的黑盒检测方法，通过截断大型语言模型的思维链过程并对比同构扰动数据，有效揭露并量化了模型因数据污染而产生的“捷径”记忆行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型的推理能力评估受到数据污染的严重威胁。由于发布者常利用重述等手段进行“逃避式”污染以刷高榜单分数，现有的检测方法难以识别此类隐蔽性污染。因此，迫切需要一种能够揭示模型通过思维链掩盖其本质记忆现象的有效检测方案。

Method: 提出了一种名为Zero-CoT Probe (ZCP)的黑盒检测方法。该方法通过强制截断模型的思维链生成过程，迫使模型直接输出答案，从而暴露出其对测试数据的潜在“捷径”式记忆；同时，通过对比原始基准数据集与同构扰动参考数据集在零思维链模式下的表现，以量化评估污染程度（Contamination Confidence）。

Result: 实验结果表明，ZCP能够稳健地检测到直接的和隐蔽的（逃避式）数据污染。相比传统方法，ZCP不仅能进行二分类判定，还能通过引入“污染置信度”指标来量化污染的严重程度，在已知污染模型及特意微调的污染模型上表现优异。

Conclusion: 通过截断思维链（CoT）来揭露大型语言模型中隐藏的数据污染现象是可行且有效的。ZCP方法提供了一种无需模型内部参数访问的黑盒检测方案，能够识别包括经过重述等逃避式策略在内的复杂数据污染，为评估LLM的真实推理能力提供了更可靠的度量手段。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated impressive reasoning abilities across a wide range of tasks, but data contamination undermines the objective evaluation of these capabilities. This problem is further exacerbated by malicious model publishers who use evasive, or indirect, contamination strategies, such as paraphrasing benchmark data to evade existing detection methods and artificially boost leaderboard performance. Current approaches struggle to reliably detect such stealthy contamination. In this work, we uncover a critical phenomenon: a model's generated reasoning steps actively mask its underlying memorization. Inspired by this, we propose the Zero-CoT Probe (ZCP), a novel black-box detection method that deliberately truncates the entire Chain-of-Thought (CoT) process to expose latent shortcut mappings. To further isolate memorization from the model's intrinsic problem-solving capabilities, ZCP compares the model's zero-CoT performance on the original benchmark against an isomorphically perturbed reference dataset. Furthermore, we introduce Contamination Confidence, a metric that quantifies both the likelihood and severity of contamination, moving beyond simple binary classifications. Extensive experiments on both previously identified contaminated models and specially fine-tuned contaminated models demonstrate that ZCP robustly detects both direct and evasive data contamination. The code for ZCP is accessible at https://github.com/Yifan-Lan/zero-cot-probe.

### [99] [When to Switch, Not Just What: Transition Quality Prediction in Clash Royale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21868)
*Heeyun Heo,Huy Kang Kim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究针对竞技游戏中玩家因连败而频繁更换策略导致表现下降的现象，提出了TQP（转换质量预测器）框架。通过综合考虑玩家个体差异、切换时机和策略预期收益，该模型显著提升了策略推荐的质量，帮助玩家减少无效切换，从而提升胜率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有策略推荐系统通常假设切换策略的成本为零，忽略了切换行为对玩家表现的负面影响及个体差异。研究发现，频繁切换策略与低胜率正相关，因此需要一种能将“策略推荐”重构为“过渡决策”的方法，以优化玩家的决策过程。

Method: 作者提出了“转换质量预测器”（TQP）三阶段流水线：
1. PersonaGate：基于玩家的个体特质，过滤掉那些因“过度切换”而导致表现下降的玩家。
2. TimingGate：利用同类状态基准对比，精准识别切换策略能带来净收益的关键时刻。
3. ScoreFusion：结合适配度信号与预测的胜率增量，对候选策略进行排名。
此外，引入了SwitchGap评估指标，在不假设玩家选择即最优的前提下，衡量推荐策略的判别质量。

Result: 分析了《皇室战争》中超过92万场比赛数据，证实了高切换频率与低胜率的负相关性。TQP模型在5.4%的推荐率下实现了+10.4个百分点的SwitchGap提升，验证了该方法在辅助玩家（尤其是易受连败影响的群体）做出理性切换决策方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究通过放弃“零切换成本假设”，证明了策略推荐应考虑玩家的切换倾向和行为成本。TQP框架有效地识别了适合切换的时间点和策略，显著提升了玩家的胜率，尤其对于那些受挫后频繁切换的低水平玩家具有重要的指导意义。

Abstract: In competitive games, players frequently switch strategies after losing streaks, yet our analysis of 926,334 match records from 34,619 Clash Royale players reveals a counterintuitive pattern: switching frequency is inversely associated with the win rate, with effects that vary substantially across players and situational contexts. We attribute this to a limitation common in many prior recommendation systems, which evaluate strategies by expected quality while overlooking the behavioral cost of switching and individual differences in switching propensity. We refer to this implicit premise as the Zero Switching Cost Assumption. To address this, we reformulate strategy recommendation as a transition-level decision problem and instantiate it as TQP (Transition Quality Predictor), a three-stage pipeline structured as Who -> When -> What. PersonaGate suppresses recommendations for players whose strategic consistency is empirically associated with superior outcomes. TimingGate identifies moments when switching is likely to yield a net benefit over staying, using a subtype- and state-matched baseline to control for natural win-rate recovery. ScoreFusion ranks candidate strategies by combining an adoptability signal with predicted transition quality (delta WR). We further introduce SwitchGap, an evaluation metric that measures a policy's discriminative quality without treating observed player choices as optimal ground truth. This property is particularly important because the most frequent switchers record the lowest win rates. The full pipeline achieves a SwitchGap of +10.4 percentage points at a recommendation rate of 5.4%, and loss-triggered switchers, despite being the lowest-performing group, benefit the most from subtype-conditioned guidance.

</details>


### [100] [Noise Schedule Design for Diffusion Models: An Optimal Control Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21911)
*Seo Taek Kong,Weina Wang,R. Srikant*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于最优控制的扩散模型噪声调度设计框架，通过最小化Fisher信息定义的误差上界，在保证理论采样效率的同时，导出了可调优的实用调度策略，提升了图像生成性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的扩散模型噪声调度大多依赖经验法则，缺乏系统性的设计框架，且现有的理论研究虽能证明采样误差上界，但对应的噪声调度方案往往不适用于实际场景。

Method: 1. 将噪声调度设计转化为基于Fisher信息演化的最优控制问题；2. 证明采样误差的KL散度上界与Fisher信息之间的函数关系；3. 利用最优控制理论推导采样误差的充分条件，并针对特定分布推导闭式解。

Result: 1. 证明了在最优噪声调度下可实现最优的采样误差上界 $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(d/n)$；2. 提出了可推广现有指数和Sigmoid调度的通用参数化调度方案；3. 实验证明通过系统调参，新调度方案在图像生成任务中取得了更优的FID指标。

Conclusion: 通过将扩散模型的噪声调度设计问题转化为最优控制问题，研究不仅在理论上推导出了最优采样误差的充分条件，还通过参数化求解得到了可调优的实用噪声调度，在图像生成基准测试中显著提升了FID得分。

Abstract: We develop a principled framework for analyzing and designing noise schedules in diffusion models. We show that one can recast this design problem as an optimal control problem, whose state is the Fisher information of the diffusion process which evolves according to an ODE and the control input is the noise schedule. The objective of the optimal control problem is a functional involving the Fisher information, which is shown to be an upper bound on the Kullback-Leibler sampling error. By solving this optimal control problem, we obtain sufficient conditions on noise schedules under which state-of-the-art $\tilde{\mathcal{O}} (d/n)$ sampling error is achievable, where $d$ is the data dimension and $n$ is the number of discretization steps. While existing theoretical work also prove that $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(d/n)$ sampling error bounds are achievable, these results hold for specific noise schedules, which do not include the schedules used in practice. Under a further parametric assumption on the data distribution, we show that one can obtain closed-form expressions for the noise schedules. These noise schedules generalize standard empirical schedules such as exponential and sigmoid schedules by allowing additional parameters that can be tuned. Systematically tuning the parameters of these schedules yields new schedules that achieve superior FID scores on image generation benchmarks.

</details>


### [101] [CausalGuard: Conformal Inference under Graph Uncertainty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21928)
*Vikash Singh,Weicong Chen,Debargha Ganguly,Yanyan Zhang,Nengbo Wang,Sreehari Sankar,Mohsen Hariri,Alexander Nemecek,Chaoda Song,Shouren Wang,Biyao Zhang,Van Yang,Erman Ayday,Jing Ma,Vipin Chaudhary*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CausalGuard 是一种将因果图结构信息与共形预测相结合的框架，利用 LLM 构建因果图先验并动态加权聚合伪结果，在观测数据中实现了更精确且具有理论覆盖保证的因果效应估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在观测数据中估计处理效应时，传统的调整集选择严重依赖于对因果图结构的先验假设。如果图结构指定错误，会导致置信区间覆盖率不足；而通用的、与图结构无关的共形预测方法往往会导致预测区间过宽（过度保守）。因此，需要一种能够结合因果结构信息并具备统计覆盖保证的鲁棒方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为 CausalGuard 的结构加权共形预测框架。该方法首先利用 LLM 获取因果图先验，结合条件独立性测试对候选有向无环图（DAG）进行剪枝，并利用贝叶斯信息准则（BIC）进行重加权；随后，通过聚合图条件的双重稳健伪结果（doubly robust pseudo-outcomes），利用复合非一致性得分进行校准，实现对条件平均处理效应（CATE）的推断。

Result: 实验结果表明，CausalGuard 在五个基准测试中均达到了 90% 以上的标称覆盖率，且在保证覆盖率的同时，显著减小了预测区间宽度，优于传统的图结构无关基准方法。该模型在处理非法对撞机调整问题及面临模型先验误差时展现了良好的稳定性。

Conclusion: CausalGuard 通过整合大语言模型（LLM）的结构先验与因果推断方法，为观测数据下的因果效应估计提供了一种稳健的、具有覆盖保证的推断框架，有效地平衡了模型偏差与统计不确定性。

Abstract: Estimating treatment effects from observational data requires choosing an adjustment set, but valid adjustment depends on an unknown causal graph. Graph misspecification can cause under-coverage, while graph-agnostic conformal wrappers may regain nominal coverage only through large padding. We introduce CausalGuard, a structure-weighted conformal framework that calibrates after aggregating graph-conditional doubly robust pseudo-outcomes. Candidate DAGs are proposed from an LLM-derived edge prior, pruned by conditional-independence tests, and reweighted by Bayesian Information Criterion. A composite nonconformity score then calibrates the posterior-weighted pseudo-outcome. CausalGuard provides distribution-free finite-sample marginal coverage for this aggregated pseudo-outcome; under causal identification, overlap, conditional-mean nuisance stability, and concentration on target-aligned valid adjustment strategies, its conditional mean converges to the true Conditional Average Treatment Effect. Across five benchmarks, CausalGuard attains mean coverage above the nominal 90% level for the directly evaluable target and reduces width when graph-agnostic conformal baselines require large padding. Stress tests show that CausalGuard suppresses invalid collider adjustment and remains stable under misspecified priors when the retained candidate set is data-supported.

</details>


### [102] [Optimal Guarantees for Auditing Rényi Differentially Private Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21938)
*Benjamin D. Kim,Lav R. Varshney,Daniel Alabi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对Rényi差分隐私（RDP）的理论最优黑盒审计框架，利用Donsker-Varadhan估计器提升了审计精度，并成功在DP-SGD算法的隐私合规性评估中实现了超越现有技术的实证结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的机器学习算法（特别是DP-SGD）声称具备Rényi差分隐私（RDP）保证，但缺乏有效的黑盒审计方法来验证这些声明的准确性，尤其是在小规模Rényi阶数下的审计精度不足。

Method: 本文提出了一种基于假设检验的审计框架，利用Donsker-Varadhan（DV）变分估计器直接估计相邻执行轨迹间的Rényi散度。通过引入类受限的DV估计器，将统计估计误差与算法隐私泄漏分离开来，并导出了显式的非渐近置信区间。同时，证明了该方法在样本复杂度上达到极小极大最优性。

Result: 实验结果表明，在MNIST和CIFAR-10数据集上，该审计框架在广泛的隐私预算范围内，显著提升了DP-SGD的RDP经验下界，在处理具有挑战性的小至中等Rényi阶数时，性能明显优于现有的黑盒审计方法。

Conclusion: 本文建立了一个针对Rényi差分隐私（RDP）的黑盒审计理论框架，证明了基于Donsker-Varadhan估计器的审计方法在样本复杂度上达到了信息论意义上的最优，并为实际评估DP-SGD等算法的隐私泄漏提供了更强有力的经验下界。

Abstract: We study black-box auditing for machine learning algorithms that claim R \ 'enyi differential privacy (RDP) guarantees. We introduce an auditing framework, based on hypothesis testing, that directly estimates Rényi divergence between neighboring executions using the Donsker-Varadhan (DV) variational estimator. Our analysis yields explicit and non-asymptotic confidence intervals for RDP auditing via class-restricted DV estimators, separating statistical estimation error from algorithmic privacy leakage. We prove matching minimax lower bounds showing that, up to logarithmic factors, our sample-complexity guarantees are information-theoretically optimal, thereby establishing the first optimal guarantees for auditing RDP via DV estimators. Empirically, we instantiate our framework for auditing DP-SGD in a fully black-box setting. Across MNIST and CIFAR-10, and over a wide range of privacy regimes, our auditors produce a strong overall improvement on empirical RDP lower bounds compared to prior state-of-the-art black-box methods especially at small and moderate Rényi orders where accurate auditing is most challenging.

### [103] [ChronoMedicalWorld: A Medical World Model for Learning Patient Trajectories from Longitudinal Care Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21963)
*Jiangyuan Wang,Xuyong Chen,Junwei He,Xu Xu,Shasha Xie,Fuman Han*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的电子健康记录（EHR）预测模型多为判别式，难以处理长期的临床模拟；而通用大语言模型在面对重复干预时容易产生预测漂移。因此，需要一个能够整合结构化数据与自由文本交流、并能模拟长期患者生理轨迹的世界模型框架。

Method: 1. 提出 CMWM 框架，采用联合嵌入状态编码器处理纵向 EHR 数据。
2. 设计宽动作编码器，融合结构化干预指标与自由文本交流嵌入。
3. 采用循环潜在转换模块，通过六项综合目标进行训练：下一观测监督、下一状态预测、SIGReg 正则化及三种生理学形状先验（斜率、连续性、大跳跃惩罚）。
4. 实施闭环滚动预测协议（closed-loop rollout-prefix protocol），确保训练目标与推理过程的一致性。

Result: 在 2,232 名慢性肾脏病（CKD）患者的队列研究中，CMWM 在年度估算肾小球滤过率（eGFR）轨迹预测任务上表现优异。相比 GPT-5.5 基准模型，CMWM 将平均绝对误差（MAE）降低了 7.28%，均方根误差（RMSE）降低了 7.35%，且模型性能的提升主要归功于对患者与健康教练交流文本的有效整合。

Conclusion: CMWM 框架通过将状态表示、多模态行动编码与生理先验约束相结合，有效解决了长期慢性病临床轨迹预测的漂移和准确性问题。该模型具有高度的泛化性，不仅适用于慢性肾脏病（CKD），还可推广至其他涉及结构化干预和自由文本交流的慢性病管理场景。

Abstract: Long-horizon clinical simulation -- predicting how a patient's physiology evolves over years under specified interventions -- is central to chronic-disease care, yet existing electronic health record (EHR) models are predominantly discriminative, and general-purpose large language models drift under repeated interventions. We propose the \textbf{ChronoMedicalWorld Model (CMWM)}, an action-conditioned latent world-model framework for learning patient trajectories from longitudinal care data. CMWM couples a joint-embedding state encoder with a wide action encoder that admits both structured intervention indicators and free-text communication embeddings, and trains a recurrent latent transition module under a six-term objective: next-observation supervision, next-latent prediction, SIGReg latent regularisation, and three physiology-aware shape priors (slope, continuity, large-jump penalty). A closed-loop rollout-prefix protocol matches training to deployment, so the model is optimised against the same multi-step error it exhibits at inference. As a concrete case study, we instantiate CMWM for annual estimated glomerular filtration rate (eGFR) trajectory forecasting in chronic kidney disease (CKD). On a 2{,}232-patient nephrology cohort, the CKD instantiation achieves a dynamic-50\% history rollout test mean absolute error (MAE) of 7.384 and root-mean-square error (RMSE) of 10.256, against 7.964 and 11.069 for a tuned GPT-5.5 structured-prompting baseline ($-7.28\%$ MAE, $-7.35\%$ RMSE), with the gain dominated by the dialogue portion of patient--health-coach communication. The framework is not CKD-specific: its architecture, loss design, and training protocol apply to any chronic condition that can be cast as periodic clinical state interleaved with structured and conversational interventions.

### [104] [An Improved Adaptive PID Optimizer with Enhanced Convergence and Stability for Deep Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21968)
*Saurabh Saini,Kapil Ahuja,Thomas Wick,Saurav Kumar*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的动量随机梯度下降存在梯度噪声和过冲现象，而 Adam 虽然解决了噪声问题却存在收敛与稳定性挑战。现有的 AdaPID 试图解决上述问题，但仍继承了 Adam 的缺陷。因此，本研究旨在通过集成先进的改进策略，构建一个既能保证快速收敛又具备高稳定性的优化器。

Method: 该研究在传统自适应 PID (AdaPID) 优化器的基础上进行了两项改进：1) 借鉴 AMSGrad 的思想，引入非递增有效学习率以解决收敛问题；2) 借鉴 DiffGrad 的思想，引入基于梯度差的调制因子以增强训练稳定性。通过结合这两项改进，形成了 IAdaPID-ADG 优化器。

Result: 在 MNIST、CIFAR10 等基准数据集以及 IARC、AnnoCerv 等真实数据集上的实验结果表明，IAdaPID-ADG 显著优于现有的主流优化器。消融实验进一步证实了所引入的两个改进组件对整体性能提升的有效性。

Conclusion: 该论文提出的 IAdaPID-ADG 优化器成功克服了现有 AdaPID 方法在收敛性和稳定性方面的缺陷，在多种基准测试和实际应用数据集上表现出优越的性能，为深度学习优化提供了一种更稳健的解决方案。

Abstract: Optimization is essential in deep learning. The foundational method upon which most optimizers are built is momentum-based stochastic gradient descent. However, it suffers from two key drawbacks. First, it has noisy and varying gradients, and second, it has an overshoot phenomenon. To address noisy gradients, Adam was proposed, which remains the most widely used adaptive optimizer. To address the overshoot phenomenon, a control-theory-based PID optimizer was proposed. To tackle both the limitations within a single framework, several variants of Adaptive PID (AdaPID) have recently been proposed.
  Although AdaPID performs well, it still inherits two critical drawbacks from Adam, namely convergence and stability issues. In this work, we address both these limitations. To fix the convergence issue, we uniquely integrate the idea of using a non-increasing effective learning rate into AdaPID (originally proposed in AMSGrad, an extension of Adam). To fix the stability issue, we innovatively integrate a gradient difference based modulation factor into AdaPID (originally proposed in DiffGrad, another extension of Adam). Combining both these ideas in AdaPID, results in our novel IAdaPID-ADG optimizer.
  We evaluate our proposed optimizer on multiple datasets, including benchmark datasets (MNIST and CIFAR10) and real-world datasets (IARC and AnnoCerv). The IAdaPID-ADG substantially outperforms all competing optimizers. Additionally, we perform an ablation study on the MNIST dataset to demonstrate the contribution of each added component.

### [105] [Reasoning through Verifiable Forecast Actions: Consistency-Grounded RL for Financial LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21975)
*Jialin Chen,Aosong Feng,Harshit Verma,Siyi Gu,Haiwen Wang,Ali Maatouk,Yixuan He,Yifeng Gao,Leandros Tassiulas,Rex Ying*

  <summary>Details</summary>

To address this, we introduce StockR1, a time-series-enhanced LLM that unifies stock forecasting and financial reasoning through a verifiable forecast action. Based on a tool-call design, the model first emits a forecast action, which is a structured and interpretable representation of its qualitative market outlook. It then invokes a time-series decoder conditioned on this action to generate distributional future trajectories, leading to more informed question answering and financial reasoning. We optimize the full pipeline with reinforcement learning, where rewards jointly reflect answer validity, forecast accuracy, and consistency between generated actions and observed time-series dynamics. In addition, rewards are reweighted by a sample-level uncertainty scalar, encouraging the model to accommodate varying uncertainty in market dynamics. We evaluate StockR1 on financial question answering and stock forecasting over a large-scale 10-year benchmark. Our method consistently outperforms time-series baselines and general-purpose LLMs, improving reasoning accuracy by 17.7% (4B) and 25.9% (8B). These findings demonstrate that structuring the forecast actions establishes a powerful synergy between language reasoning and temporal prediction, enabling LLMs to reason through verifiable, interpretable, and numerically grounded decisions.

### [106] [Check Your LLM's Secret Dictionary! Five Lines of Code Reveal What Your LLM Learned (Including What It Shouldn't Have)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22005)
*Hisashi Miyashita*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于权重矩阵SVD分析的大语言模型审计技术。仅需几行代码，无需模型推理，即可直接从权重中提取可解释的语义子空间，从而揭示模型训练数据的偏见、安全隐患以及分词特征，为LLM的透明度与安全性审计提供了一种轻量级且强大的新工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM审计方法通常需要昂贵的推理计算或复杂的探测手段。研究者旨在探索一种仅通过分析静态权重矩阵就能直接揭示模型内部语义结构、训练数据构成及潜在不安全内容的方法，以提升模型安全性与可解释性。

Method: 利用奇异值分解（SVD）直接分析大型语言模型（LLM）的输出层（lm_head）权重矩阵。通过分析左奇异向量所对应的词表聚类，识别模型内部的语义子空间；引入“词表聚类评分（VCS）”来量化子空间一致性，并利用“加权投影评分（WPS）”实现无需模型推理的静态异常（glitch）令牌检测。

Result: 研究发现，不同模型（如GPT, Gemma, Qwen）在奇异值谱和词表聚类结构上表现出显著差异；SVD分析能揭示模型预训练数据中的不当内容且发现这些内容在后训练对齐阶段难以被完全消除；此外，WPS方法成功检测到了已知异常令牌，证明了该方法在安全审计中的有效性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，对Transformer模型输出层（lm_head）权重矩阵进行奇异值分解（SVD）是一种高效、无需推理的审计方法，能够揭示模型的语义结构、训练数据偏见及潜在的毒性内容。作者建议将该方法标准化，作为LLM发布前的安全审计步骤，并为优化分词器和设计可控模型提供了新思路。

Abstract: We show that singular value decomposition of the lm_head} weight matrix of a transformer-based large language model -- requiring only five lines of PyTorch and no model inference -- reveals interpretable semantic subspaces directly from the model weights. Each left singular vector identifies the vocabulary tokens most readily selected when the hidden state aligns with the corresponding singular direction; inspecting these clusters exposes the model's training data composition and curation philosophy.
  Analysing GPT-OSS-120B, Gemma-2-2B, and Qwen2.5-1.5B, we find that singular value spectra and vocabulary cluster structures differ systematically across models: GPT exhibits a graduated hierarchy of functionally differentiated subspaces; Gemma is dominated by pre-nineteenth-century English orthography, forming a stepwise clustering structure that may contribute to high output controllability; and Qwen exhibits broad multilingual coverage alongside subspaces whose vocabulary the authors have determined to be ethically inappropriate for direct publication.
  Base-instruct comparison reveals that ethically concerning subspaces originate in pretraining and are not removed by post-training alignment. We introduce the Vocabulary Cluster Score (VCS) to quantify subspace coherence, and the Weighted Projection Score (WPS) as a static glitch token detector; applying WPS to GPT-OSS-120B recovers shokubutsu-hyakka-tsu (ID 137606), a well-known glitch token widely reported in the CJK language community, without any model inference. We propose a taxonomy of root causes for problematic vocabulary content and call for lm_head} SVD analysis to be adopted as a standard pre-release safety auditing step. Our findings further suggest directions toward SVD-guided tokenizer optimisation and more controllable LLM design.

### [107] [CASE-NET: Deep Spatio-Temporal Representation Learning via Causal Attention and Channel Recalibration for Multivariate Time Series Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22043)
*Fan Zhang,Yating Cui,Hua Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对多变量时间序列分类中因果缺失和噪声干扰的问题，本文提出了 CASE-NET 架构，通过结合因果时间编码与自适应通道重校准技术，实现了更优的特征表示和分类性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多尺度多变量时间序列分类模型存在两个主要瓶颈：一是标准编码器缺乏因果性，导致在非平稳动态中产生时间混淆；二是缺乏显式的通道显著性机制，容易导致噪声污染潜在空间。

Method: 提出了一种名为 CASE-NET 的架构，主要包含两个核心模块：1. 因果时间编码器（Causal Temporal Encoder），利用掩码自注意力机制和因果卷积强制执行物理时间箭头约束；2. 自适应通道重校准模块（Adaptive Channel Recalibration），作为信息瓶颈来抑制噪声，突出重要通道特征。

Result: 在六个异构数据集上进行了全面评估，CASE-NET 在其中四个任务上刷新了最高水平（SOTA），在 AWR 数据集上达到了 98.6% 的峰值准确率，并在非平稳环境下表现出卓越的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: CASE-NET 通过因果约束和通道自适应机制，有效地解决了多变量时间序列分类中的时间混淆和噪声污染问题，为处理非平稳动态数据提供了一种鲁棒且高效的新范式。

Abstract: Multivariate time series (MTS) classification is foundational to pervasive computing and financial analysis, yet existing multi-scale paradigms are often constrained by suboptimal representation fidelity. We identify two critical bottlenecks: temporal non-causality in standard encoders that induces temporal confounding in non-stationary dynamics, and the absence of explicit channel saliency mechanisms that allows noise to contaminate the latent space. To address these challenges, we propose the Causal Attention and Spatio-temporal Encoder Network (CASE-NET), an architecture designed for structural manifold pre-conditioning. CASE-NET synergizes a Causal Temporal Encoder, which enforces physical arrow-of-time constraints via masked self-attention and causal convolutions, with an Adaptive Channel Recalibration module functioning as an information bottleneck to suppress detrimental noise. Comprehensive evaluations across six heterogeneous domains demonstrate that CASE-NET establishes new state-of-the-art benchmarks on four tasks, achieving a peak accuracy of 98.6% on the AWR dataset and superior robustness in non-stationary regimes.

### [108] [LABO: LLM-Accelerated Bayesian Optimization through Broad Exploration and Selective Experimentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22054)
*Zhuo Chen,Xinzhe Yuan,Jianshu Zhang,Jinzong Dong,Ruichen Zhou,Yingchun Niu,Tianhang Zhou,Yu Yang Fredrik Liu,Yuqiang Li,Nanyang Ye,Qinying Gu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LABO是一种新型贝叶斯优化框架，通过引入门控机制智能平衡大模型预测与真实实验，在保障科学发现质量的同时大幅提升了样本效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学探索中实验成本高昂且数据匮乏，现有将大语言模型嵌入贝叶斯优化的方法未能充分利用大模型低成本评估的优势，导致采样效率有待提升。

Method: 提出了一种名为LABO的框架，将大语言模型（LLM）的廉价预测与真实实验观察整合在同一贝叶斯优化（BO）循环中，并设计了一个门控准则（gating criterion）来动态平衡模型预测与实际实验的权重。此外，还通过累积遗憾界（cumulative regret bound）证明了该方法的效率提升。

Result: 在多种科学任务的实证中，LABO在相同实验预算下表现优于现有方法，验证了其在样本效率和优化性能上的显著优势。

Conclusion: LABO通过在贝叶斯优化框架中动态整合大语言模型预测，有效降低了实验成本并提高了采样效率，为将大模型集成到科学发现流程中提供了理论支持与实践范式。

Abstract: The high cost and data scarcity in scientific exploration have motivated the use of large language models (LLMs) as knowledge-driven components in Bayesian optimization (BO). However, existing approaches typically embed LLMs directly into the sampling or surrogate modeling pipeline, without fully leveraging their significantly lower evaluation cost compared to real-world experiments. To address this limitation, we propose LLM-Accelerated Bayesian Optimization (LABO), a framework that combines LLM predictions with experimental observations within a single BO loop. LABO employs a gating criterion to dynamically balance the reliance on LLM predictions versus actual experiments. By leveraging inexpensive LLM evaluations to broadly explore the search space and reserving costly real experiments only for regions with high uncertainty, LABO achieves more sample-efficient optimization. We provide a theoretical analysis with a cumulative regret bound that formalizes this efficiency gain. Empirical results across diverse scientific tasks demonstrate that LABO consistently outperforms existing methods under identical experimental budgets. Our results suggest that LABO offers a practical and theoretically grounded approach for integrating LLMs into scientific discovery workflows.

### [109] [Prototype-Guided Classification Sub-Task Decoupling Framework: Enhancing Generalization and Interpretability for Multivariate Time Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22055)
*Xianhao Song,Yuang Zhang,Yuqi She,Liping Wang,Xuemin Lin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PDFTime是一种新型的原型引导时间序列分类框架，通过将直接的黑盒分类映射重构为多阶段的相似性推理过程，实现了特征提取与决策逻辑的解耦，在保持高准确度的同时提升了模型的可解释性。

Method: 提出了一种名为PDFTime的原型引导框架，将时间序列分类重新定义为多阶段的决策过程。该方法不再依赖传统的直接特征到标签的映射，而是利用学习到的原型（Prototypes）在潜在空间中逼近类条件特征分布，通过不同粒度的分类子任务实现逐步判别，从而解耦了特征提取与决策逻辑。

Result: PDFTime在UEA和UCR基准测试中取得了最先进（SOTA）的性能。特别是在UCR数据集的128个数据集测试中，PDFTime在80个数据集上获得了第一名的准确率，在一致性和泛化能力上均显著优于现有的主流基准模型。

Conclusion: PDFTime通过引入原型引导的多阶段决策机制，成功打破了传统时间序列分类中“黑盒”映射的范式。该研究证明了将特征提取与决策逻辑解耦，不仅能显著提升分类准确率，还能为模型提供更好的可解释性，为时间序列分析领域提供了一种新的通用建模范式。

Abstract: Time Series Classification (TSC) is a long-standing research problem that has gained increasing attention in recent years with the rapid growth of large-scale temporal data. Despite substantial progress enabled by deep learning, designing TSC models that are both accurate and interpretable remains a challenging task. Many existing approaches adopt a direct feature-to-label classification paradigm, by collapsing high-dimensional temporal embeddings into class logits via a single linear projection (often after global pooling), the paradigm conflates feature extraction and decision logic into an inseparable mapping.
  To address these limitations, we propose PDFTime, a prototype-guided framework that reformulates time series classification as a multi-stage decision process. Instead of direct feature-to-label mapping, PDFTime leverages learned prototypes to approximate class-conditional feature distributions in the latent space, enabling progressive discrimination through classification sub-tasks of varying granularity. To our knowledge, PDFTime is the first framework to reformulate time series classification as a decoupled, multi-stage similarity-based reasoning process, breaking the long-standing paradigm of direct, black-box feature-to-label mapping. Extensive evaluations demonstrate that PDFTime achieves state-of-the-art (SOTA) performance across UEA and UCR benchmarks. Notably, it secures the top-$1$ accuracy on 80 out of 128 datasets in the UCR archive, significantly outperforming recent strong baselines in both consistency and generalization.

### [110] [From Reasoning Chains to Verifiable Subproblems: Curriculum Reinforcement Learning Enables Credit Assignment for LLM Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22074)
*Xitai Jiang,Zihan Tang,Wenze Lin,Yang Yue,Shenzhi Wang,Gao Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SCRL是一种新的课程强化学习框架，通过将复杂数学推理问题拆解为多个可验证的子问题，并利用子问题级奖励归一化技术进行细粒度信用分配，显著提升了大语言模型在处理高难度推理任务时的学习效率和准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于结果的强化学习（RLVR）在大语言模型处理高难度推理问题时存在效率低下问题，主要原因是正确答案的采样极其稀缺，且基于样本级别的信用分配无法有效利用失败尝试中的部分正确推理步骤。

Method: 1. 子问题课程构建：基于参考推理链推导出可验证的子问题序列，并将原问题作为最终子问题，将复杂问题转化为课程学习任务；2. 子问题级奖励归一化：在每个子问题位置独立归一化奖励，计算优势并分配给相应的答案片段，实现细粒度的信用分配。

Result: SCRL在七个数学推理基准测试中表现优异，在Qwen3-4B-Base模型上相较于GRPO基线平均准确率提升4.1个百分点，在Qwen3-14B-Base上提升1.9个百分点；在AIME24、AIME25及IMO-Bench等高难度数据集上，SCRL进一步提升了模型的探索能力和解题准确率。

Conclusion: SCRL通过将复杂推理问题分解为一系列可验证的子问题，并结合细粒度的信用分配机制，有效解决了强化学习在硬推理任务中探索效率低和奖励稀疏的问题，为提升大语言模型的数学推理能力提供了一种高效且无需额外奖励模型的通用方案。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR) has shown strong promise for LLM reasoning, but outcome-based RLVR remains inefficient on hard problems because correct final-answer rollouts are rare and sample-level credit assignment cannot use partial progress in failed attempts. We introduce SCRL (Subproblem Curriculum Reinforcement Learning), a curriculum RL framework that derives verifiable subproblems from reference reasoning chains and fixes the final subproblem as the original problem. This turns partial progress on hard problems into verifiable learning signals. Algorithmically, SCRL uses subproblem-level normalization, which normalizes rewards independently at each subproblem position and assigns the resulting advantages to the corresponding answer spans, enabling finer-grained credit assignment without external rubrics or reward models. Our analysis shows that subproblem curricula lift hard problems out of gradient dead zones, with larger relative gains as the original problem becomes harder. Across seven mathematical reasoning benchmarks, SCRL outperforms strong curriculum-learning baselines, improving average accuracy over GRPO by +4.1 points on Qwen3-4B-Base and +1.9 points on Qwen3-14B-Base. On AIME24, AIME25, and IMO-Bench, SCRL further improves pass@1 by +3.7 points and pass@64 by +4.6 points on Qwen3-4B-Base, indicating better exploration on hard reasoning problems.

### [113] [Short-Term-to-Long-Term Memory Transfer for Knowledge Graphs under Partial Observability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22142)
*Taewoon Kim,Vincent François-Lavet,Michael Cochez*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对强化学习记忆管理的神经符号化框架，通过学习显式的决策策略来决定哪些观测信息应进入长期记忆库，在有限存储空间下实现了优于传统基线模型的记忆效率和可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种神经符号化、基于值函数的决策框架。该方法将观测到的三元组视为潜在的记忆项，利用基于项（per-item）的Q学习和共享参数设计，评估每个三元组保留至长期记忆库的价值。通过时间差分（TD）更新机制，在处理变长短期缓冲区的同时，显式决定记忆的留存与遗忘。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了在部分可观测的强化学习任务中，通过神经符号化的决策机制对观测信息进行显式筛选（保留或丢弃），能有效提升长期记忆的利用效率。这种基于项的Q学习方法为在有限记忆空间内维持高价值历史信息提供了一种可解释且高效的途径。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning under partial observability requires deciding what information to retain, yet most memory-based approaches do not explicitly model short-term-to-long-term transfer of symbolic observations. We study this transfer process in a temporal knowledge-graph memory setting and cast it as a neuro-symbolic value-based decision problem: for each observed triple, the agent chooses whether to keep or drop it before long-term insertion. To handle variable-sized short-term buffers, we use a per-item Q-learning design with shared parameters and a practical temporal-difference update over matched items across consecutive steps. On the RoomKG benchmark at long-term memory capacity 128, learned transfer decisions outperform symbolic and neural baselines, including symbolic baselines with temporal annotations and history-based LSTM/Transformer baselines. Across transfer-policy ablations, a lightweight local short-term-only variant performs best, and step-level behavior shows that the policy keeps navigation- and query-relevant facts while discarding lower-value candidate facts, supporting explicit and interpretable memory decisions under memory constraints.

### [114] [Algebraic Machine Learning for Small-to-Medium Datasets Is Competitive against Strong Standard Baselines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22155)
*David Mendez,Fernando Martin-Maroto,Gonzalo G. de Polavieja*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于代数结构的子直接分解（subdirect decomposition）理论，而非传统的基于梯度下降的数值优化。该方法不需要交叉验证来调整超参数，依赖于通用的代数归纳偏置，而非针对特定数据模态（如图像或表格）的特定偏差。

Result: 在50-2000个训练样本的小至中等规模数据集上，AML在图像分类任务中表现优于包括CNN在内的基准方法；在表格数据任务中，尽管XGBoost表现最优，但AML仍能与LightGBM和随机森林等强基准模型相媲美。此外，AML完全无需超参数调优即可达到上述性能。

Conclusion: 代数机器学习（AML）作为一种无需数值优化且具备通用归纳偏置的符号学习方法，在小样本数据集上展现出了极强的竞争力和鲁棒性，证明了符号方法在无需超参数调优的情况下也能与现代深度学习模型媲美。

Abstract: Symbolic methods are generally not considered competitive with strong modern learners on realistic supervised tasks. We evaluate Algebraic Machine Learning (AML), a framework that learns through subdirect decomposition of algebraic structure rather than numerical optimization, against standard baselines on image and tabular classification across varying training-set sizes. We find that AML trained only on training data without using validation or cross-validation outperforms a family of cross-validated baseline methods including CNNs on small to medium image datasets (50--2000 training examples). On tabular datasets in the same size range, XGBoost is overall the best performing method, but AML is nonetheless comparable to methods incorporating task-specific biases such as LightGBM and random forests. AML achieves this competitive performance across two very different types of datasets using a generic algebraic inductive bias, rather than the modality-specific biases built into standard baselines like CNNs for images or XGBoost for tabular data, and requires no cross validation because it has no task-dependent hyperparameters to tune.

### [115] [One-Way Policy Optimization for Self-Evolving LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22156)
*Shuo Yang,Jinda Lu,Kexin Huang,Chiyu Ma,Shaohang Wei,Yuyang Liu,Guoyin Wang,Jingren Zhou,Li Yuan*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的强化学习与可验证奖励（RLVR）方法在通过代币级约束稳定训练时，往往会不加区分地惩罚所有偏离参考策略的行为，导致模型在尝试超越参考策略时受到抑制，降低了推理能力的扩展效率。

Method: 提出单向策略优化（OWPO）方法，核心是解耦优化方向与更新幅度。通过非对称重加权技术，对落后于参考策略的偏差进行“加速对齐”，对超越参考策略的偏差进行“增益锁定”，并引入迭代式参考更新机制以巩固性能增益。

Result: 实验结果表明，OWPO 在性能上显著优于 DAPO、OPD 和 MOPD 等强基准方法，打破了固定先验的瓶颈，使模型能够实现持续的自我进化。

Conclusion: OWPO 通过解耦优化方向与更新幅度，有效解决了 RLVR 中传统约束方法抑制模型性能提升的问题，并通过“棘轮效应”实现了大语言模型推理能力的持续自我进化，无需依赖固定的外部参考模型。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has become a promising paradigm for scaling reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs). However, the sparsity of binary verifier rewards often leads to low efficiency and optimization instability. To stabilize training, existing methods typically impose token-level constraints relative to a reference policy. We identify that such constraints penalize deviations indiscriminately; this can flip verifier-determined direction when the policy attempts to outperform the reference, thereby suppressing gains. To resolve this, we propose One-Way Policy Optimization (OWPO), a method based on the principle of decoupling optimization direction from update magnitude. In OWPO, the verifier dictates the update direction, while the reference policy serves only to adjust the magnitude. Specifically, OWPO applies asymmetric reweighting: it performs Accelerated Alignment for inferior deviations (where the policy lags behind the reference) and Gain Locking for superior deviations (where the policy surpasses the reference). Furthermore, by incorporating iterative reference updates, OWPO creates a ``Ratchet Effect'' that continuously consolidates gains. Experimental results demonstrate that OWPO outperforms strong baselines, including DAPO, OPD, and MOPD, breaking the bottleneck of fixed priors to enable continuous self-evolution without reliance on external reference models.

</details>


### [116] [Maestro: Reinforcement Learning to Orchestrate Hierarchical Model-Skill Ensembles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22177)
*Jinyang Wu,Guocheng Zhai,Ruihan Jin,Yuhao Shen,Zhengxi Lu,Fan Zhang,Haoran Luo,Zheng Lian,Zhengqi Wen,Jianhua Tao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Maestro是一个基于强化学习的智能体编排框架，通过动态调度多个专家模型和技能库，实现了比单一顶级大模型更高效、更强大的多模态任务解决能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的智能体框架过度依赖单一的大型语言模型，难以充分利用不同模型在各自擅长领域（如数学推理、感知分析等）的优势，限制了任务执行的上限。

Method: 提出Maestro框架，将多模态任务建模为基于分层模型-技能注册表的序列决策过程。使用强化学习（RL）训练一个轻量级（4B）编排策略，动态决定每一步是否调用外部专家、选择哪个模型-技能对以及何时终止任务，无需步骤级的监督。

Result: 在十个多模态基准测试中，Maestro仅使用4B规模的编排器就达到了70.1%的平均准确率，超过了GPT-5（69.3%）和Gemini-2.5-Pro（68.7%）；且具备极强的泛化能力，无需重训练即可集成未见过的新模型和技能。

Conclusion: Maestro证明了通过强化学习驱动的动态编排，无需依赖单一的大型全能模型，即可通过组合多个冻结的专家模型和技能库来实现超越顶级闭源模型的性能。该方法具有极高的灵活性和可扩展性，为构建高效的多模态智能体提供了新范式。

Abstract: The proliferation of large language models (LLMs) and modular skills has endowed autonomous agents with increasingly powerful capabilities. Existing frameworks typically rely on monolithic LLMs and fixed logic to interface with these skills. This gives rise to a critical bottleneck: different LLMs offer distinct advantages across diverse domains, yet current frameworks fail to exploit the complementary strengths of models and skills, thereby limiting their performance on downstream tasks. In this paper, we present Maestro (Multimodal Agent for Expert-Skill Targeted Reinforced Orchestration), a Reinforcement Learning (RL)-driven orchestration framework that reframes heterogeneous multimodal tasks as a sequential decision-making process over a hierarchical model-skill registry. Rather than consolidating all knowledge into a single model, Maestro trains a lightweight policy to dynamically compose ensembles of frozen expert models and a two-tier skill library, deciding at each step whether to invoke an external expert, which model-skill pair to select, and when to terminate. The policy is optimized via outcome-based RL, requiring no step-level supervision. We evaluate Maestro across ten representative multimodal benchmarks spanning mathematical reasoning, chart understanding, high-resolution perception, and domain-specific analysis. With only a 4B orchestrator, Maestro achieves an average accuracy of 70.1%, surpassing both GPT-5 (69.3%) and Gemini-2.5-Pro (68.7%). Crucially, the learned coordination policy generalizes to unseen models and skills without retraining: augmenting the registry with out-of-domain experts yields a 59.5% average on four challenging benchmarks, outperforming all closed-source baselines. Maestro further maintains high computational efficiency with low latency. The source code is available at https://github.com/jinyangwu/Maestro.

### [117] [Beyond Euclidean Proximity: Repairing Latent World Models with Horizon-Matched Trajectory Reachability Metrics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22164)
*Liangyu Li,Shengzhi Wang,Qingwen Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对潜空间模型预测控制中终端代价度量失效的问题，本文提出轨迹可达性度量（TRM），通过引入长时程监督的成对排序机制，显著提升了机器人在复杂任务中的规划成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在潜空间模型预测控制（MPC）中，通常使用潜在空间中终端状态与目标状态之间的欧几里得距离来评估候选轨迹。然而，这种简单的距离度量往往无法正确捕捉与任务达成相关的关键变量（如空间位置），导致规划器选出错误的轨迹。作者旨在修复这一终端代价接口问题，以改善规划器在长时程和复杂任务中的决策质量。

Method: 提出轨迹可达性度量（TRM），这是一种用于固定潜在世界模型的后验终端排序方法。核心方法包括：1. 训练一个小型成对预测头，利用已记录的轨迹结构进行监督学习；2. 采用“视野感知（horizon-aware）”训练策略，通过平衡时间间隔的样本对齐长时程终端排序需求；3. 将该度量作为原有的终端代价（terminal cost）的替代或混合方案，无需重新训练原有的编码器、动力学模型或采样器。

Result: 在TwoRoom基准测试中，基于LeWM的规划成功率从7.0%提升至97.0%；在PLDM基准上，成功率从32.7%提升至84.0%。分析显示，尽管潜在空间中XY位置可线性解码，但原始MSE度量无法有效排序，而TRM成功提取了关键的可达性信号，优化了规划器对终端节点的选择。

Conclusion: 轨迹可达性度量（TRM）为现有潜在世界模型提供了一种有效的后验优化方案。研究表明，仅依靠潜在空间中的欧几里得距离往往会误导规划器，而通过引入针对长时程设计的成对判别头，可以显著提升规划在复杂环境（如TwoRoom和PushT）中的成功率，证明了针对目标导向规划进行显式度量学习的必要性。

Abstract: Latent world models can contain the state needed for control, yet their terminal-cost interface can expose the planner to the wrong decision-relevant information. In common latent MPC, candidate sequences are ranked by Euclidean distance between predicted terminal and goal latent states; this assumes that raw latent distance weights reachability-relevant variables correctly. We propose trajectory reachability metrics (TRM), a post-hoc terminal-ranking method for fixed latent world models. TRM trains a small pairwise head from logged trajectory structure and uses it as a replacement or hybrid cost; the encoder, dynamics, sampler, optimizer, and evaluation manifests remain fixed. The key design choice is horizon-aware supervision: the metric is trained on broad, balanced temporal separations to match the long-horizon terminal candidate ranking problem. On a hard TwoRoom benchmark, raw latent planning with LeWorldModel (LeWM) reaches 7.0% success, while full-horizon TRM reaches 97.0%; shuffled temporal-label controls stay at 0.0%. The same recipe improves a PLDM baseline from 32.7% to 84.0% across three seeds, and a short-horizon TRM variant reaches only 35.0% with the 100,000 pair budget. In TwoRoom, we provide mechanistic evidence for why TRM works: XY position is linearly decodable (R^2=0.998), yet raw latent MSE misranks candidates; the XY-probe rowspace accounts for less than 1% of terminal-goal latent MSE but carries most candidate-quality signal; and SCSA audits show that TRM improves the ordering and selected endpoint seen by the planner. On PushT go50/go75, TRM-style task-state metrics improve SCSA ranking and selected final distance more cleanly than closed-loop success, motivating auxiliary hybrid costs in continuous manipulation. TRM is the planner-facing repair, and audits explain when terminal reachability metrics should replace or augment raw latent proximity.

### [118] [Survive or Collapse: The Asymmetric Roles of Data Gating and Reward Grounding in Self-Play RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22217)
*Sophia Xiao Pu,Zhaotian Weng,Chengzhi Liu,Jayanth Srinivasa,Gaowen Liu,William Yang Wang,Xin Eric Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究揭示了自我博弈强化学习崩溃的根本原因在于缺乏有效的数据门控，而非奖励函数设计不当。通过控制实验证实，严格的数据筛选机制是保障系统稳定性的关键因素，甚至优于依赖地面真实值的奖励优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自我博弈强化学习在提升语言模型推理能力方面表现出色，但普遍存在训练崩溃与不稳定性问题。学界目前多将此归因于奖励设计（Reward-design）问题，本研究旨在探讨是否存在更根本的机制——即数据层面的筛选逻辑——来决定自我博弈的稳定性。

Method: 研究采用受控实验方法，在 Python 输出预测任务及确定性 DSL（领域特定语言）任务上进行了对比实验。研究者将自我博弈系统解构为“数据门控”与“奖励信号”两个杠杆，并通过剥离预训练先验、输出歧义和执行器噪声，评估了不同门控严格度与奖励变体对模型稳定性的影响。

Result: 实验发现，门控与奖励的作用是不对称的：即使在没有地面真实值（ground truth）的自洽性奖励下，严格的门控也足以维持稳定性；反之，若缺乏门控，任何奖励变体都无法防止崩溃。此外，引入连续的门控严格度参数（ε）揭示了训练指标与验证准确率之间的两阶段相变现象。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，数据门控机制（Data-level gating）是自我博弈强化学习稳定性的核心约束，而非奖励函数的校准。此外，该研究揭示了“有根据的提议者悖论”，即过强的提议者在缺乏有效门控时，反而会加速模型收敛到虚假的自洽吸引子，导致性能崩溃。

Abstract: Self-play reinforcement learning trains language models on their own generated tasks, co-evolving a proposer and solver without human labels. Recent systems report strong reasoning gains, but collapse and instability are widely observed and poorly understood. The dominant response treats this as a reward-design problem. We argue instead that self-play stability is governed by two distinct levers: a data-level gate that decides which proposer-generated tasks enter the training pool, and the reward signal that updates the policy on tasks already admitted. Through controlled experiments on a Python output-prediction task and a deterministic-DSL twin task that strips pretraining priors, output ambiguity, and executor noise, we find the two levers are asymmetric. A strict gate is sufficient for stability under every reward variant we test, including a self-consistency reward with no access to ground truth; while no reward variant is sufficient once the gate is removed. This asymmetry exposes a counter-intuitive coupling we call the Grounded Proposer Paradox: a proposer with ground-truth access accelerates collapse faster than an ungrounded one when paired with a self-consistency solver, by concentrating training on clean tasks that form the fastest path to a spurious self-consistent attractor. Replacing the binary gate with a continuous strictness parameter $\varepsilon$ further reveals a two-stage phase transition: training-side metrics decouple at low $\varepsilon$, while validation accuracy holds until $\varepsilon$ is much higher. Data-level gating, not reward calibration, is the binding constraint on self-play stability.

### [119] [Boundary-targeted Membership Inference Attacks on Safety Classifiers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22373)
*Anthony Hughes,Alexander Goldberg,Prince Jha,Adam Perer,Nikolaos Aletras,Niloofar Mireshghallah*
