TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种新型攻击方法，通过识别安全分类器在训练数据边界上的低置信度样本，成功揭示了心理健康数据在模型训练过程中的隐私泄露风险，并证明了该攻击方法远超现有同类技术。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式AI的安全分类器通常在包含自残、心理健康等敏感话题的数据集上训练，存在显著的隐私泄露隐患。现有的成员推理攻击（MIA）尚未深入探讨安全分类器在处理敏感数据时的脆弱性，研究旨在量化并验证基于置信度边界的攻击方式对隐私的威胁。

Method: 提出了一种“边界靶向选择策略”（boundary-targeted selection strategy）。该方法通过定位分类器置信度最低的样本，利用模型对训练数据中模糊部分的“记忆”特性，放大成员身份泄露的信号，从而执行成员推理攻击（MIA）。

Result: 实验结果显示，在检测用户心理困扰的分类器上，该攻击方法能在5%的误报率下成功恢复19%的训练对话数据，其性能比现有先进的MIA方法高出3.5倍。此外，研究还验证了现有的噪声添加策略能够有效缓解此类边界样本的隐私风险。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了安全分类器在处理敏感数据时存在的隐私泄露风险，证明了基于置信度边界的攻击策略比现有方法更有效。研究建议通过噪声注入等防御策略来减轻这种脆弱性，并指出单纯的内容过滤无法解决此类隐私问题。

Abstract: Safety classifiers are essential safeguards within generative AI systems, filtering harmful content or identifying at-risk users when interacting with large language models. Despite their necessity, these models are trained on sensitive datasets including discussions of self-harm and mental health, raising important, yet poorly understood, privacy concerns. Membership inference attacks (MIAs) allow adversaries to infer membership of examples used to train models. In this work, we hypothesize that identifying the examples on which the classifier is least confident are informative for an adversary to infer membership. This reflects a localized failure of generalization, where the model relies on memorization to resolve ambiguity in the training set. To investigate this, we introduce a new boundary-targeted selection strategy that identifies low confidence examples that amplify the signal of an examples membership within a training set. Our experimental results show that an adversary can recover 19\% of the conversations a safety classifier flagged as indicating user distress, at a 5\% false-positive rate, on a classifier fine-tuned for detecting a user who may require emotional support. This is $3.5$ times more than attacking using state-of-the-art MIA methods alone. Finally, we characterize the boundary laying examples and show that content-based filtering is ineffective for protection, and existing noise strategies can effectively mitigate susceptibility of these examples.

### [120] [IKNO: Infinite-order Kernel Neural Operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22182)
*Pengyuan Zhu,Ivor W. Tsang,Yueming Lyu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出无穷阶核神经算子（IKNO），通过引入高阶核积分增强了算子的表达能力，并设计了高效的快速计算算法，实现了在科学计算任务中精度与计算效率的双重领先。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的神经算子主要依赖于一阶核积分近似，这极大地限制了其模型表达能力。为了提升算子捕捉复杂函数映射的能力，研究人员寻求一种能够利用更高阶信息且具备高效计算特性的神经算子构建方法。

Method: 提出无穷阶核神经算子（IKNO），包含两种实现方式：1. IKNO-Vanilla，通过Kronecker特征分解在乘积网格上应用全核预解算子；2. IKNO-TP，一种组合各轴预解算子的张量积算子。同时，作者为这两种变体设计了快速计算方案，以确保在处理大规模数据时的计算效率。

Result: 实验表明，IKNO在多个与时间相关及无关的基准数据集上均达到SOTA性能。特别是在处理具有任意输入形状的大规模工业数据集时，IKNO不仅显著提升了预测精度，还保持了极高的计算可扩展性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的无穷阶核神经算子（IKNO）通过引入无穷阶核积分，有效克服了传统一阶核积分在表达能力上的限制，并证明了其在计算效率和泛化性能上的卓越表现，代表了神经算子领域在复杂科学计算任务中的新SOTA。

Abstract: Neural operators have achieved significant success in modern scientific computing due to their flexibility and strong generalization capabilities. Existing models, however, primarily rely on first-order kernel integral approximations, which severely limit their expressivity. To address this, we propose the Infinite-order Kernel Neural Operator (IKNO), which constructs neural operators via infinite-order kernel integrals and admits an elegant closed-form finite approximation. We develop two complementary infinite-order neural operator constructions: IKNO-Vanilla, which applies the full-kernel resolvent on the product grid via Kronecker eigendecomposition, and IKNO-TP, an alternative tensor-product operator that composes per-axis resolvents. Furthermore, we develop fast computation schemes for both variants of IKNO, which achieve outstanding global information aggregation while maintaining high computational efficiency. Empirically, we evaluate our IKNO on both time-dependent and time-independent benchmarks with arbitrary input shapes, including large-scale industrial datasets. Extensive experiments demonstrate that the IKNO method consistently achieves the SOTA accuracy with significant improvements on nearly all benchmark datasets while maintaining scalability to very large point clouds.

Method: 提出了一种通用的CPU-GPU异构计算框架，通过批量化处理BnB节点，利用轻量级自定义内核和填充（padding）技术处理非规则数据结构，将复杂的BnB运算转化为GPU高效的矩阵与并行操作。

Abstract: GPUs have significantly accelerated first-order methods for large-scale optimization, especially in continuous optimization. However, this success has not transferred cleanly to problems with discrete variables, combinatorial structure, and nonlinear objectives, such as certifying optimal solutions for cardinality-constrained generalized linear models. Major challenges include the sequential processing of heterogeneous nodes in branch and bound (BnB) and frequent data movement between the CPU and GPU. We propose a simple, generic, and modular CPU--GPU framework that processes multiple BnB nodes in batches on GPUs. The framework is built around a small set of GPU-efficient routines and uses padding together with lightweight custom kernels to handle irregular node data structures. Experiments show one to two orders of magnitude speedups and zero optimality gap on challenging instances. The framework can also be extended to collect the entire Rashomon set, enabling downstream statistical analysis such as variable-importance analysis and model selection under secondary user-specific measures (e.g., AUC in classification).

### [122] [Structured-Sparse Attention for Entity Tracking with Subquadratic Sequence Complexity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22476)
*Hangyue Zhao,Paul Caillon,Erwan Fagnou,Alexandre Allauzen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对Transformer在长序列追踪任务中的计算瓶颈，该论文提出了一种利用注意力稀疏结构（块对角分布）的快速评估算法，显著降低了计算复杂度并提升了实际运行速度，同时指出了注意力头数对多属性追踪能力的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Transformer模型在处理长序列实体追踪任务时，全注意力计算开销过大。尽管现有的多跳状态传播机制可以减少层数，但其稠密计算仍导致高昂的运算成本。研究旨在利用注意力矩阵的结构稀疏性来优化计算流程，在不牺牲精度的前提下提升长序列的处理效率。

Method: 研究通过分析发现注意力权重高度集中在块对角区域，提出了一种“块状评估（blockwise evaluation）”方法，利用解算子式（resolvent-style）算子将块内交互精确化，同时通过精简系统处理跨块交互，从而降低了计算复杂度。

Result: 该方法将序列长度的复杂度降低至 $O(n^{4/3}d)$。在受控追踪基准测试中，其在达到与稠密算子相同精度的情况下，墙上时钟时间缩短了 12-29%；与紧凑型稠密Transformer相比，在同等准确率下速度提升高达 2.4 倍。此外，研究发现当并发属性数量超过注意力头数时，模型性能会显著下降。

Conclusion: 该研究证实了通过利用注意力机制的块对角结构特性，可以在保持模型精度的同时显著提升长序列实体追踪任务的计算效率。该方法不仅在理论上达到了次二次复杂度，还在实际应用中证明了其在计算性能上的优势，同时也揭示了模型容量与注意力头数之间存在的关键性能瓶颈。

Abstract: Entity tracking requires maintaining and updating latent states for entities and attributes over long sequences. Recent task-specific attention operators can compress deep Transformer stacks into a few layers by performing multi-hop state propagation within a single layer, but their dense evaluation remains expensive. We show that in this setting, learned attention is strongly structured: most mass concentrates in local block-diagonal neighborhoods with a light cross-block residue. Exploiting this, we derive a blockwise evaluation of a resolvent-style operator that keeps within-block interactions exact and routes cross-block interactions through a reduced system. The resulting evaluation is subquadratic in sequence length $O(n^{4/3}d)$ (and $O(n^{7/3})$ when $d\approx n$). On controlled tracking benchmarks, our method matches the dense operator's accuracy while reducing wall-clock time by $12-29\%$ under a standardized measurement protocol, and is up to $2.4 \times$ faster than a compact dense Transformer at comparable exact-match accuracy. We further provide ablations over block size and model capacity, and identify a limitation: performance collapses when the number of simultaneously evolving properties exceeds the number of attention heads.

</details>


### [123] [Bandit Convex Optimization with Gradient Prediction Adaptivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22191)
*Shuche Wang,Adarsh Barik,Vincent Y. F. Tan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了带梯度预测的赌博机凸优化（BCO）。研究指出单点反馈无法通过预测显著优化 regret；为此提出了 TP-VR-OPT 算法，在两点反馈下通过方差缩减实现了与预测误差相关的最优遗憾界，并将其推广至非平稳环境。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究在带梯度预测的赌博机凸优化（BCO）中，预测是否能以“预测自适应”的方式改善最坏情况下的遗憾（regret）界。针对当前梯度估计方差较大导致预测优势被掩盖的问题，探索如何在反馈限制下利用预测信息提升学习效率。

Method: 1. 理论分析：证明了在单点反馈协议下，即使预测误差较小，仍存在 Ω(√T) 的遗憾下界。
2. 算法设计：提出“两点方差缩减乐观梯度下降”（TP-VR-OPT）算法，引入一种方差随预测误差而非梯度范数缩减的新型梯度估计器。
3. 扩展：开发了无需预知预测误差或时间跨度的自适应变体，并将其扩展至非平稳环境以保证动态遗憾。

Result: 1. 证明了单点反馈下，遗憾下界 Ω(√T) 难以摆脱。
2. 在两点反馈模型下，算法 TP-VR-OPT 实现了 O(√d·E[S_T]) 的遗憾界，其中 d 为维度，S_T 为累积预测误差。
3. 给出了信息论意义下的下界 Ω(√E[S_T])，证明了所提算法的次优性（仅差 √d 因子）。
4. 验证了算法在自适应和非平稳环境下的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了在带梯度预测的赌博机凸优化中，单点反馈模型存在不可逾越的 regret 下界，而通过两点反馈并结合提出的 TP-VR-OPT 算法，可以实现预测自适应的 regret 界。研究结果表明，该算法在理论上接近最优，并能有效处理非平稳环境。

Abstract: Bandit convex optimization (BCO) is a fundamental online learning framework with partial feedback, where the learner observes only the loss incurred at the chosen decision point in each round. In this work, we investigate whether optimistic gradient predictions can improve worst-case regret guarantees in a prediction-adaptive manner. Specifically, given gradient predictions $m_t$, we seek regret bounds that scale with the cumulative prediction error $S_T=\sum_{t=1}^T \|\nabla f_t(x_t)-m_t\|^2.$ We first establish a negative result: under the single-point feedback protocol, an unavoidable $Ω(\sqrt{T})$ regret lower bound persists even when $S_T=o(T)$, showing that the variance of gradient estimation fundamentally obscures the benefit of accurate predictions. To overcome this barrier, we propose \emph{Two-Point Variance-Reduced Optimistic Gradient Descent} (TP-VR-OPT) for the two-point feedback setting. The key idea is a novel variance-reduced gradient estimator whose variance scales with the prediction error rather than the gradient norm. This yields a regret bound of $O\big(\sqrt{d\,\mathbb{E}[S_T]}\big),$ where $d$ is the decision dimension. Complementing this result, we establish an information-theoretic lower bound that scales as $Ω(\sqrt{\mathbb{E}[S_T]})$, providing a fundamental characterization of the best achievable prediction-adaptive regret and showing that TP-VR-OPT is optimal up to a factor of $\sqrt d$. We further develop adaptive variants that eliminate the need for prior knowledge of $\mathbb{E}[S_T]$ or the horizon $T$, and extend our framework to non-stationary environments, establishing dynamic regret guarantees that adapt simultaneously to the cumulative prediction error and the comparator path length.

</details>

*Manuel Noah Riesen,Peter Alfred von Niederhäusern*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的“思维图”（GoT）框架虽能有效处理复杂问题，但其操作图结构通常需要人工预先定义，缺乏灵活性，难以应对多样化任务中对不同推理路径的适配需求。因此，研究者旨在通过自动化方式使思维图结构更具适应性和灵活性。

Method: 提出“强化思维图”（Reinforced Graph of Thoughts, RGoT）框架，通过引入强化学习（RL）机制，使得大语言模型能够根据任务复杂度，从预定义的操作集合中自动、自适应地构建和优化思维操作图，克服了原有GoT方法依赖人工手动设计固定图结构的局限性。

Abstract: Graph of Thoughts (GoT), a generalized form of recent prompting paradigms for large language models (LLMs), has been shown to be useful for elaborate problem solving. By executing a graph of operations, thoughts of the LLM are structured as an arbitrary graph, forming the actual graph of thoughts. Originally, the graph of operations is defined manually, which requires in-depth knowledge about the solution of the problem to solve. Such a static graph of operations is rigid and therefore lacks adaptability. We propose Reinforced Graph of Thoughts (RGoT), an automated approach to the GoT prompting paradigm that leverages reinforcement learning (RL) to adaptively generate a graph of operations from a human-defined set. ### [125] [A Tutorial on Diffusion Theory: From Differential Equations to Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22586)
*Jiayi Fu,Yuxia Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在从微分方程的数学角度系统性地梳理和推导扩散模型，以消除不同模型表述间的混淆，并为扩散模型的训练、采样及引导技术提供统一的理论框架。

Method: 通过微分方程视角构建扩散模型，推导了前向过程的ODE与SDE表示，利用边缘分数的反向动力学进行推导，并论证了噪声预测目标函数与分数匹配的等价性。此外，还涵盖了包括DPM-Solver在内的采样方法及引导式采样技术。

Result: 成功证明了扩散模型的前向过程可转化为ODE/SDE动力学；论证了标准的噪声预测目标函数等价于分数匹配；并明确了DDPM和DDIM分别是离散化的反向SDE和反向ODE采样实现。

Conclusion: 本教程统一了扩散模型的数学框架，证明了DDPM和DDIM等模型本质上都是基于分数匹配（score matching）的微分方程求解过程，为理解和开发生成模型提供了坚实的理论基础。

Abstract: This tutorial develops diffusion models from the viewpoint of differential equations. We begin with the conditional Gaussian forward process and show that this path admits both an ordinary differential equation (ODE) representation and a stochastic differential equation (SDE) representation. Averaging the conditional process over the data distribution then yields marginalized forward ODE and SDE formulations that transport the data distribution $p_0=p_{\mathrm{data}}$ to a Gaussian prior $p_1=\mathcal{N}(0,I)$. We next derive the corresponding reverse-time dynamics, namely the reverse SDE and the reverse probability-flow ODE, both of which are governed by the marginal score $\grad\log p_t(x)$. This leads to a training objective for score estimation and shows that the standard noise-prediction objective is equivalent to score matching up to an additive constant independent of the model parameters. We then discuss sampling methods for the learned reverse dynamics, including DPM-Solver, as well as guided sampling through classifier guidance and classifier-free guidance. Finally, we compare DDPM and DDIM with the reverse SDE/ODE framework and show that they share the same training objective, while DDPM sampling corresponds to discrete reverse-SDE sampling and DDIM sampling corresponds to reverse-ODE sampling.

### [126] [Two is better than one: A Collapse-free Multi-Reward RLIF Training Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22620)
*Shourov Joarder,Diganta Sikdar,Ahsan Habib Akash,Binod Bhattarai,Prashnna Gyawali*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种多奖励RLIF框架，通过组合答案级投票与token级自确信度奖励，并配合KL-Cov正则化与GDPO归一化，有效解决了无监督强化学习中常见的奖励劫持与熵坍缩问题，在无需外部监督的前提下实现了高质量的长程推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的RLIF方法通常依赖单一的内部奖励，这容易导致奖励劫持、熵坍缩以及推理结构的退化。此外，传统的强化学习方案高度依赖人工标注或标准答案，缺乏可扩展性，因此需要一种更稳定、无需外部监督的替代方案。

Method: 提出了一种多奖励内部反馈强化学习（RLIF）框架，包含两部分：1. 基于聚类投票的答案级奖励与基于token级自确信度的完成级奖励；2. 采用基于GDPO的归一化方法处理奖励尺度不平衡；3. 引入KL-Cov正则化机制，旨在防止模型后期出现熵坍缩，保持探索能力。

Result: 在数学推理和代码生成基准测试中，该方法相比以往的无监督强化学习方法表现出更高的稳定性和鲁棒性，且其性能表现接近于有监督的RLVR方法。

Conclusion: 本文证明了通过整合互补的内部奖励信号并辅以针对性的正则化技术，可以在无需外部监督的情况下，显著提升大型语言模型在长程推理任务中的稳定性和性能，为无监督强化学习路径提供了有效的优化范式。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has substantially improved the reasoning ability of LLMs, but often depends on external supervision from human annotations or gold-standard solutions. Reinforcement learning from internal feedback (RLIF) has recently emerged as a scalable unsupervised alternative, using signals extracted from the model itself. However, existing RLIF methods typically rely on a single internal reward, which can lead to reward hacking, entropy collapse, and degraded reasoning structure. We propose a multi-reward RLIF framework that decomposes the training signal into two complementary components: an answer-level reward based on cluster voting and a completion-level reward based on token-wise self-certainty. To combine these signals robustly, we apply GDPO-based normalization to reduce reward-scale imbalance. We further introduce KL-Cov regularization, which targets low-entropy token distributions responsible for disproportionate entropy reduction, preserving exploration and preventing late-stage collapse. Across mathematical reasoning and code-generation benchmarks, our method improves stability and robustness over prior unsupervised RL approaches, while achieving performance close to supervised RLVR methods. These results show that complementary internal rewards, combined with targeted regularization, can support stable long-horizon reasoning without relying on external ground-truth supervision. Code will be released soon.

### [127] [Can Transformers Learn to Verify During Backtracking Search?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22221)
*Yin Jun Phua,Tony Ribeiro,Tuan Nguyen,Katsumi Inoue*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究并解决了Transformer在搜索树推理中对历史路径过度依赖的问题，通过引入SSA注意力掩码机制，确保模型决策仅基于当前状态，提升了推理逻辑的准确性和一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的Transformer搜索模型通常通过在离线轨迹数据上进行自回归训练，但这种方式存在局限性：最优的搜索策略（继续或回溯）应仅取决于当前状态，而非达成该状态的历史路径。该研究旨在解决模型在处理累积轨迹时无法实现这一原则的问题。

Method: 1. 诊断了Transformer在累积轨迹数据上的缺陷，包括状态特征在序列中分散（分散检索）以及模型过度依赖决策路径而非当前状态（历史纠缠）。
2. 提出“局部化（Localization）”方法：重写决策块，将状态特征集中暴露在局部。
3. 提出“选择性状态注意力（SSA）”：通过固定的注意力掩码结构，强制模型仅关注当前状态，无需修改训练数据、目标函数或参数。

Result: 在3-SAT、图着色、块世界和回溯解析等任务中，对比传统的累积训练因果基准模型，使用SSA机制的模型在仅历史路径不同但状态相同的测试用例中，能够保持决策的一致性，有效消除了历史路径对决策的干扰。

Conclusion: 本研究表明，基于Transformer的搜索模型在处理累积轨迹数据时会受限于“分散检索”和“历史纠缠”问题。通过引入局部化策略和选择性状态注意力（SSA）机制，可以强制模型基于当前状态而非历史轨迹做出决策，从而提升推理的鲁棒性和一致性。这一发现对于提升大型语言模型在搜索与推理任务中的性能具有重要意义。

Abstract: Backtracking search underlies classical constraint solvers, planners, and theorem provers. Recent transformer-based reasoning systems explore search trees over their own intermediate steps. A common training recipe fits an autoregressive next-token loss on offline solver traces. The model's input at each step is a cumulative trace of all prior decisions. The optimal continue-or-backtrack predictor depends only on the current search state, since two trajectories reaching the same state admit the same viable continuations. We show that decoder-only transformers trained on cumulative traces fail this requirement in two ways: the trace can scatter state features across many positions (scattered retrieval), and the predictor can condition on the trajectory rather than the state (history entanglement). We address scattered retrieval with localization, a trace-level fix that rewrites each decision block to expose state features locally. We address history entanglement with Selective State Attention (SSA), a fixed attention mask that enforces state-based decisions structurally without modifying training data, objective, or parameters. We focus on reactive verification, after propagation has exposed a contradiction. We test SSA on 3-SAT, graph coloring, Blocks World, and backtracking parsing. On same-state pairs that differ only in prior history, SSA emits identical decisions while a cumulative-trained causal baseline does not. Our contribution is a diagnostic of transformer behavior on serialized trajectory data, paired with a structural fix. Pretrained language models that search over their own reasoning steps may face the same failure. Our analysis opens up inference-time context clearing as a candidate way to apply the same isolation without retraining.

</details>


### [128] [ARC-STAR: Auditable Post-Hoc Correction for PDE Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22222)
*Chengze Li,Lingwei Wei,Li Sun,Hongbo Lv,Jie Yang,Hongrong Zhang,Kening Zheng,Wei-Chieh Huang,Enze Ma,Philip S. Yu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ARC-STAR 是一种针对 PDE 基础模型的后处理框架，通过分层校正与自适应计算分配，在保持预训练模型不变的情况下，显著降低了流体模拟的预测误差并提高了计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 偏微分方程（PDE）基础模型在处理未见流场时存在预测漂移和误差空间集中问题。现有的重训练方法容易导致模型不稳定，而统一的后处理手段忽略了误差的空间分布差异，因此需要一种既能保持预训练模型、又能自适应解决局部高误差区域的修正方法。

Method: 提出了 ARC-STAR（自适应风险校准空间分类审计修正）框架，该框架包含三个核心阶段：1. 全局校正器：消除广义求解器偏差；2. 块级局部精炼器：处理全局校正后的残差；3. 部署阶段的标签无关评分机制：根据计算预算将资源动态分配至高风险区域。该方法无需对基础模型进行微调，实现了审计性与计算预算的平衡。

Result: 在五个流体基准测试的十个实验场景中，ARC-STAR 均能将速度演化误差降低至少 36 倍。具体而言，全局阶段减少了 91%-99% 的原始误差，后续的局部精炼阶段进一步消减了剩余残差的 94.4%。

Conclusion: ARC-STAR 框架为 PDE 基础模型提供了一种高效、模块化且可解释的后处理修正方案。通过分阶段的偏差消除和高风险区域自适应优化，该方法在保持预训练模型权重冻结的前提下，显著提升了流体动力学预测的精度与鲁棒性。

Abstract: Partial differential equation (PDE) foundation models are pretrained networks that forecast how physical fields like velocity and pressure evolve from a single reusable solver. On unfamiliar flows their predictions drift step by step, errors concentrate in a few regions, yet retraining destabilizes the network and uniform post-hoc correction overlooks this spatial concentration. To address this, we propose a frozen-solver post-hoc correction framework, Adaptive Risk-Calibrated Spatial Triage for Auditable Refinement (ARC-STAR). ARC-STAR organizes correction into three stages: a global corrector removes broad solver bias, a blockwise local refiner cleans the post-global residual, and, at deployment, a label-free score routes refinement to high-risk blocks under a compute budget. The framework is designed to be (i) frozen-host, preserving the pretrained solver without fine-tuning; (ii) auditable, with global and local stages trained and evaluated separately for measurable contributions; and (iii) budget-aware, using a blockwise interface that either refines the full field or routes limited compute to high-risk regions. Across five flow benchmarks spanning ten regime cells, ARC-STAR is the only method that cuts velocity rollout error by at least 36x over raw Poseidon on every cell. The global stage reduces raw host error by 91-99%, and the local stage further reduces the remaining post-global residual by up to 94.4%. Our code implementation is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/arc_star.

### [129] [How Many Different Outputs Can a Transformer Generate?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22223)
*Maxime Meyer,Mario Michelessa,Caroline Chaux,Vincent Y. F. Tan*

TL;DR: 该论文定量分析了Transformer架构对模型输出能力的影响，揭示了其在处理简单序列任务时存在本质的长度上限，并从数学上证明了可访问序列随提示词长度的线性约束及指数级衰减规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在理解Transformer模型为何在处理简单的序列任务（如复制和机械记忆）时表现出已知的性能瓶颈，并通过分析其架构特征来量化模型能够输出的序列数量。

Method: 1. 理论建模：推导了基于Transformer架构特性的可访问序列数量的上界。
2. 经验验证：在多种架构和不同模型规模上，验证了模型预测结果与实际输出能力的紧密程度。
3. 数学证明：证明了可访问序列长度与提示词长度的线性关系，以及在超过临界阈值后可访问序列比例的指数衰减规律。

Result: 1. 提出了一个受提示词长度限制的紧致上界（误差因子小于10）。
2. 证明了可访问序列的最大长度与提示词长度成线性比例。
3. 发现超过特定临界点后，可访问序列的比例随序列长度呈指数级下降。
4. 提供了一个理论上限来界定提示词长度与可访问序列长度之间的线性系数。

Conclusion: 研究表明Transformer的输出能力受到其架构特性的严格限制。即使在无限上下文和计算时间的理想条件下，其可生成序列的长度也存在理论上限，且该上限随提示词长度呈线性增长。这揭示了Transformer在处理复制或记忆等简单序列任务时存在根本性的能力瓶颈。

Abstract: We study how we can leverage only a handful of characteristics of a transformer's architecture to closely predict the number of different sequences it can output, both qualitatively and quantitatively. We provide an upper bound depending on the length of the prompt, which we show empirically to be tight up to a factor less than 10, across architectures and model sizes. Our analysis also provides a theoretical explanation for previously observed empirical failures of transformers on simple sequence tasks, such as copying and cramming. Formally, we prove that (i) the maximal length of accessible sequences (those that the transformer can output for some prompt) grows linearly with the prompt length, (ii) beyond a critical threshold, the proportion of accessible sequences decays exponentially with sequence length, and (iii) the linear coefficient relating prompt length to accessible sequence length admits a theoretical upper bound. Notably, these results hold even with unbounded context and computation time.

</details>


### [130] [Vector Policy Optimization: Training for Diversity Improves Test-Time Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22817)
*Ryan Bahlous-Boldi,Isha Puri,Idan Shenfeld,Akarsh Kumar,Mehul Damani,Sebastian Risi,Omar Khattab,Zhang-Wei Hong,Pulkit Agrawal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 为了解决传统强化学习中单一奖励优化导致模型多样性不足的问题，本文提出了向量策略优化（VPO），通过显式训练模型生成多样化的解决方案以应对下游复杂的向量奖励，显著提升了模型在推理时搜索和进化搜索任务中的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大型语言模型后训练范式主要依赖于单一标量奖励优化，导致模型生成的响应分布熵较低，缺乏多样性，无法满足推理时搜索（如 AlphaEvolve）对多样化解空间的需求，进而限制了模型在复杂任务中的推理能力。

Method: 提出了一种名为向量策略优化（Vector Policy Optimization, VPO）的强化学习算法。VPO 将传统的标量奖励扩展为向量奖励（如代码生成的多个测试用例准确率或多用户画像），通过替换 GRPO 中的优势估计器，引导模型学习生成多样化的解决方案，使不同的响应能够适应向量奖励空间中不同的权衡维度。

Result: 在四项任务的测试中，VPO 在推理时搜索指标（如 pass@k 和 best@k）上表现出与现有最强标量强化学习基线相当或更优的性能，且随着搜索预算的增加，优势更加明显。特别是在进化搜索任务中，VPO 使模型能够解决 GRPO 无法处理的复杂问题。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，在推理时搜索（如进化搜索）日益标准化的背景下，将“多样性优化”作为后训练的核心目标至关重要。VPO 通过矢量奖励机制成功突破了传统标量优化带来的低熵分布限制，为大型语言模型在复杂、多目标任务中的表现提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Language models must now generalize out of the box to novel environments and work inside inference-scaling search procedures, such as AlphaEvolve, that select rollouts with a variety of task-specific reward functions. Unfortunately, the standard paradigm of LLM post-training optimizes a pre-specified scalar reward, often leading current LLMs to produce low-entropy response distributions and thus to struggle at displaying the diversity that inference-time search will require. We propose Vector Policy Optimization (VPO), an RL algorithm that explicitly trains policies to anticipate diverse downstream reward functions and to produce diverse solutions. VPO exploits that rewards are often vector-valued in practice, like per-test-case correctness in code generation or, say, multiple different user personas or reward models. VPO is essentially a drop-in replacement for the GRPO advantage estimator, but it trains the LLM to output a set of solutions where individual solutions specialize to different trade-offs in the vector reward space. Across four tasks, VPO matches or beats the strongest scalar RL baselines on test-time search (e.g. pass@k and best@k), with the gap widening as the search budget grows. For evolutionary search, VPO models unlock problems that GRPO models cannot solve at all. As test-time search becomes more standardized, optimizing for diversity may need to become the default post-training objective.

### [131] [Decomposing Ensemble Spread in Lorenz '96 With Learned Stochastic Parameterizations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22242)
*Birgit Kühbacher,Daan Crommelin,Niki Kilbertus*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究利用Lorenz 1996模型分析了天气与气候集合预报中离散度不足的问题，证明了具备时间持久性的随机参数化方法能有效提升预报的离散度与误差一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 天气和气候预报因混沌特性、初始条件误差和物理过程描述不完整而存在不确定性。现有的集合预报系统普遍存在离散度不足（underdispersive）的问题，即预报离散度增长速度无法匹配预报误差，本研究旨在解析这一现象的成因并提出改进策略。

Method: 研究人员采用了Lorenz 1996双尺度系统作为受控实验平台，系统性地分离了内在变率、初始条件扰动及随机模型不确定性。实验对比了多种集合配置和参数化策略，涵盖了确定性方法、自回归方法以及新型的贝叶斯和流模型（flow-based）方法。

Result: 研究结果表明，集合扰动并不能增加系统的长期方差，而是调控了轨迹去相关和探索不变测度的速率。具有时间持久结构的随机参数化方案能显著提升早期离散度的增长，并有效提高离散度与误差之间的一致性。

Conclusion: 本研究通过解构不同不确定性来源（初始条件扰动与模型不确定性），阐明了它们在混沌系统中的交互机制。结论指出，随机参数化（尤其是具有时间持久结构的方案）对于改善集合预报的离散度不足至关重要，并为未来天气和气候模型的随机方案设计提供了明确的指导。

Abstract: Weather and climate forecasts are inherently uncertain due to chaotic dynamics, imperfect initial conditions, and incomplete representation of the underlying physical processes. Operational ensemble forecasts aim to represent these uncertainties through forecast spread, yet many approaches yield underdispersive estimates, with spread that grows too slowly relative to forecast error. Using the two-scale Lorenz 1996 system as a widely used, controlled testbed, we design a systematic approach to disentangle intrinsic variability, initial-condition perturbations, and stochastic model uncertainty. We compare multiple ensemble configurations and parameterization strategies, including existing deterministic and autoregressive as well as novel Bayesian and flow-based approaches. Our results show that ensemble perturbations do not increase the system's long-term variance; rather, they regulate how rapidly trajectories decorrelate and explore the invariant measure. Stochastic parameterizations, particularly those with temporally persistent structure, enhance early spread growth and improve spread-error consistency. Overall, we bring clarity to how different sources of uncertainty interact in a chaotic system and provide guidance for the design and evaluation of stochastic parameterizations in weather and climate models.

Abstract: Predictive modelling is important for health data analysis and data-driven clinical decision-making. All recommendations were supported by existing literature. The method also proved effective on two additional public datasets, demonstrating wider applicability. The proposed Exploratory AI Recommender demonstrates the potential of explainable AI and data-driven study design to improve the process of developing, and the performance of high-dimensional transparent predictive models.

### [133] [What are the Right Symmetries for Formal Theorem Proving?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22257)
*Krzysztof Olejniczak,Radoslav Dimitrov,Xingyue Huang,Bernardo Cuenca Grau,Jinwoo Kim,İsmail İlkan Ceylan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对LLM形式化定理证明器对问题描述高度敏感的问题，本文提出了“重写范畴”理论框架，定义了证明的对称性属性，并提出一种测试时聚合方法，通过利用问题的等价重写来提升证明器的鲁棒性与性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前基于大语言模型（LLM）的形式化定理证明器对问题表述的微小变动极度敏感，即语义等价但表述不同的问题会导致证明成功率的巨大差异，这表明模型缺乏对数学中固有结构对称性的理解，从而限制了证明器的性能和鲁棒性。

Method: 1. 提出“重写范畴（rewriting categories）”的范畴论框架，用于形式化证明策略带来的转换；2. 定义了证明等变性（proof equivariance）和成功不变性（success invariance）两个对称性概念；3. 评估并对比了状态驱动证明器与LLM证明器在这些属性上的差异；4. 提出测试时聚合方法（test-time aggregation），即对输入问题的不同等价表述进行推理聚合，以逼近成功不变性。

Result: 实证结果表明，现有的LLM证明器并不满足证明等变性或成功不变性；所提出的测试时聚合方法在理论上证明了其在采样极限下可恢复成功不变性，并在实验中验证了该方法能有效提升模型在固定推理预算下的鲁棒性和证明成功率。

Conclusion: 研究表明，对称性是当前基于LLM的定理证明器中缺失的关键归纳偏置。通过在测试时引入针对等价重写的聚合方法，可以有效弥补这一缺陷，从而提升证明器的鲁棒性和整体性能，为解决形式化数学中的表示敏感性问题提供了有效路径。

Abstract: Formal theorem provers based on large language models (LLMs) are highly sensitive to superficial variations in problem representation: semantically equivalent statements can exhibit drastically different proof success rates, revealing a failure to respect structural symmetries inherent in formal mathematics. This raises a central question: what are the right symmetries for formal theorem proving? We introduce rewriting categories, a category-theoretic framework capturing the compositional, generally non-invertible transformations induced by proof tactics, and use it to formalize two symmetry notions: proof equivariance, governing how proof distributions transform under rewrites, and success invariance (i.e., invariance of success probability), requiring equivalent statements to be solved with the same probability. We observe that state-based next-tactic provers naturally satisfy proof equivariance by operating on proof states. In contrast, state-of-the-art LLM-based provers satisfy neither property, exhibiting large performance variation across equivalent formulations. To mitigate this, we propose test-time methods that aggregate over equivalent rewritings of the input, showing theoretically that they recover success invariance in the sampling limit, and empirically, that they improve robustness and performance under fixed inference budgets. Our results highlight symmetry as a key missing inductive bias in LLM-based theorem proving and suggest test-time computation as a practical route to approximate it.

Third, all levels of the evidence hierarchy are used to craft a Bayesian threat type classification mechanism with domain knowledge-informed priors. ### [135] [Tailoring Teaching to Aptitude: Direction-Adaptive Self-Distillation for LLM Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22263)
*Hongbin Zhang,Chaozheng Wang,Kehai Chen,Youcheng Pan,Yang Xiang,Jinpeng Wang,Min Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为DASD的自适应自我蒸馏方法，通过根据模型预测的熵值动态决定是否参考特权信息，解决了大模型自我蒸馏中“探索能力受损”和“执行稳定性差”之间的矛盾，显著提升了数学推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的在线自我蒸馏（OPSD）范式通过使用“特权信息”作为引导进行token级监督，虽然能提高单步执行准确度，但会抑制模型的预测不确定性，导致模型在复杂推理任务中丧失探索和假设修正能力，从而造成整体性能退化。

Method: 作者提出了“方向自适应自我蒸馏”（DASD）。该方法核心思想是根据模型在各token处的预测熵值动态调整监督方向：当熵值高时，抑制模型对教师的盲目模仿以保留探索空间；当熵值低时，强制模型向教师对齐以确保执行的稳定性。

Result: 在六个数学推理基准测试中，DASD的表现优于现有的强化学习（RLVR）和传统自我蒸馏基线模型。实验表明，DASD在保持高推理健康度（reasoning health）和泛化能力的同时，显著提升了Avg@16指标。

Conclusion: DASD通过将自我蒸馏从简单的“强制对齐”转化为“基于熵的差异化监督”，有效解决了现有在线自我蒸馏方法中存在的探索能力受损问题。该研究证明了在模型训练中动态调整对教师建议的依赖程度对于提升复杂推理能力至关重要，为大语言模型的推理强化提供了一种更高效的范式。

Abstract: On-policy self-distillation (OPSD) is an emerging LLM post-training paradigm in which the model serves as its own teacher: conditioned on privileged information such as a reference trace or hint, the same policy provides dense token-level supervision on its own rollouts. However, recent studies show that OPSD degrades complex reasoning by suppressing predictive uncertainty, which supports exploration and hypothesis revision. Our token-level analysis shows that this failure arises from applying a uniform direction of teacher supervision across tokens with different uncertainty levels: conformity to the privileged self-teacher suppresses exploration at high entropy, while deviation from the teacher degrades step accuracy at low entropy. Accordingly, we propose \textbf{Direction-Adaptive Self-Distillation} (\textbf{DASD}), which reframes privileged self-distillation from uniform teacher imitation into entropy-routed directional supervision: high-entropy tokens are pushed away from the privileged teacher to preserve exploration, while low-entropy tokens are pulled toward the teacher to stabilize step-level execution. Across six mathematical reasoning benchmarks, DASD achieves the best macro Avg@16 over strong RLVR and self-distillation baselines. Pass@$k$, reasoning-health, and generalization analyses show that these average gains come from preserving exploration without sacrificing step-level execution.

### [136] [Detecting Atypical Clients in Federated Learning via Representation-Level Divergence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22266)
*Cristian Pérez-Corral,Jose I. Mestre,Alberto Fernández-Hernández,Manuel F. Dolz,Enrique S. Quitana-Ortí*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于输入空间激活分区变化的轻量级几何指标，用于量化联邦学习中客户端的函数偏差，以识别异常更新并优化模型聚合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联邦学习中客户端数据异构（non-i.i.d.）不仅导致全局模型性能下降，还可能引发分布偏移或异常输入，使得传统的聚合策略在面对非典型或恶意客户端更新时变得不可靠，因此迫切需要一种方法来量化和区分客户端的函数偏差。

Method: 提出了一种轻量级的几何信号方法。该方法不直接比较模型参数或梯度，而是通过共享的探测数据集（probe set），衡量本地训练如何改变模型对输入空间的激活分区（activation-induced partition），从而量化客户端与全局模型的函数偏差。该指标具有置换不变性和可解释性。

Result: 实验表明，该几何信号能够有效识别导致非典型函数变化的客户端，并将正常的异构客户端与显著偏离全局规律的异常更新区分开来。该工具可直接用于联邦学习中的客户端行为监控和风险感知聚合。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种基于几何信号的客户端行为量化方法，通过监控模型决策边界的演变，为联邦学习系统提供了更具解释性和鲁棒性的客户端评估与风险感知聚合手段。

Abstract: Federated learning enables collaborative training across distributed clients with heterogeneous data, but such heterogeneity often leads to unstable updates and degraded global performance. Moreover, in practical deployments, client updates may deviate from the expected behavior not only due to benign not i.i.d. distributions, but also due to distributional shifts or anomalous inputs, raising concerns about the reliability of the aggregation process. In this work, we propose a lightweight geometric signal to quantify the functional deviation of a client with respect to the global model. Instead of comparing model parameters or gradients, our approach measures how the local training of each client alters the activation-induced partition of the input space, evaluated on a shared probe set. This yields a permutation-invariant, interpretable metric of client--global divergence that captures differences in how data is processed by the model. We show that this signal effectively identifies clients that induce atypical functional changes, distinguishing stable yet heterogeneous clients from those whose updates significantly diverge from the global regime. As a result, the proposed metric provides a simple tool for monitoring client behavior and enabling risk-aware aggregation strategies in federated learning systems.

### [137] [Adaptive Measurement Allocation for Learning Kernelized SVMs Under Noisy Observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22275)
*Artur Miroszewski*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对量子机器学习等场景中核矩阵获取受限且带有噪声的问题，该论文提出了一种任务感知的自适应测量分配策略，通过量化核矩阵项对分类决策的影响，将测量资源集中于“决策关键区域”，有效提升了核支持向量机的性能并降低了测量成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的核方法假设核矩阵是精确且无噪声的，但在量子机器学习等新兴领域，核矩阵项需通过受限的测量预算从噪声数据中推断。目前的均匀分配策略虽然平衡了估计方差，却忽视了核化分类器对核矩阵各部分贡献的不均匀依赖性，导致测量资源浪费，限制了学习精度。

Method: 提出了一种针对噪声伯努利观测的自适应测量分配策略，主要包含两个核心原则：1. 几何敏感性（Geometric Sensitivity）：捕捉核矩阵各项扰动对分类器边界的影响；2. 活动集不稳定性（Active-set Instability）：量化测量噪声导致支持向量成员发生离散变化的可能性。基于这两个信号，动态地将有限的测量预算集中于对决策至关重要的区域。

Result: 理论分析确定了自适应分配优于均匀分配的条件，即取决于核重要性结构的异质性。合成数据和真实世界数据（量子核）的实验表明，在固定测量预算下，该策略显著改善了支持向量恢复、边界估计和决策函数准确度；同时，通过提出的稳定性准则可实现高效的提前终止机制，仅需少量测量成本即可达到接近最优的性能。

Conclusion: 研究表明，自适应测量分配策略能够显著提升在噪声环境（如量子机器学习）下的核SVM学习效果。该方法通过量化核矩阵对分类决策的敏感度，打破了传统的均匀分配范式，证明了在特定核结构异质性条件下，自适应策略优于均匀策略，并可通过双系数稳定性准则实现测量预算的高效利用。

Abstract: Kernel methods are typically formulated under the assumption of exact, noise-free access to the Gram matrix. However, in emerging settings such as quantum machine learning, each kernel entry must be inferred from noisy observations, and its accuracy depends on how a limited measurement budget is allocated. Despite this, existing approaches overwhelmingly rely on uniform allocation, which equalizes estimator variance but ignores the highly non-uniform dependence of kernelized classifiers on the Gram matrix. In this work, we introduce an adaptive measurement-allocation strategy for learning kernelized Support Vector Machines (SVMs) from noisy Bernoulli observations. Our approach combines two complementary principles: (i) geometric sensitivity, capturing how perturbations of individual kernel entries affect the classifier margin, and (ii) active-set instability, quantifying the probability of discrete changes in support-vector membership induced by measurement noise. These signals define a task-aware allocation scheme that concentrates measurements on the most decision-critical regions of the kernel matrix. We provide a theoretical analysis showing that the benefit of adaptive allocation is governed by the heterogeneity of the induced kernel importance structure, leading to distinct regimes in which adaptive or uniform strategies are preferable. Empirical evaluations on synthetic datasets demonstrate that adaptive allocation significantly improves support-vector recovery, margin estimation, and decision-function accuracy under fixed measurement budgets. A dual-coefficient stability criterion further enables early stopping, achieving near-optimal performance while using only a fraction of the measurement cost. Additional experiments on quantum kernels derived from real-world data reveal a regime-dependent behavior aligned with known phenomena such as kernel concentration. Together...

### [138] [EmoTrack: Robust Depression Tracking from Counseling Transcripts across Session Regimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22286)
*Zhaomin Wu,Jiayi Li,Bingsheng He*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对文本咨询中抑郁症监测难的问题，提出了 EmoTrack 框架。该框架融合了大模型临床信号提取、逐句语义嵌入和跨会话记忆机制，在单次及多次会话预测任务中均显著提升了 PHQ-8 评分的预测准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于微调的方法在数据稀缺时泛化能力较差，而基于提示学习的大语言模型方法往往难以有效处理多会话的纵向上下文信息，导致在实际心理咨询场景中对抑郁症严重程度（PHQ-8）的预测不够稳健。

Method: 提出了 EmoTrack 框架：1) 利用大语言模型提取临床特征并结合冻结的逐句语义嵌入；2) 构建症状特异性预测器；3) 引入紧凑的跨会话记忆机制，以处理多会话中的长期上下文信息。同时发布了多会话咨询数据集 LongCounsel。

Result: 在 DAIC-WOZ 基准测试中，EmoTrack 实现了 13.5% 的 MAE 相对降低；在 LongCounsel 数据集上，该方法在处理多次咨询会话的追踪任务中表现出极强的竞争力和鲁棒性。

Conclusion: EmoTrack 通过结合大语言模型的临床信号提取能力与长程记忆机制，有效解决了文本咨询中抑郁症严重程度评估在单次和多次会话场景下的鲁棒性问题，为心理健康AI监测提供了高效且可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: Text-based counseling is an important interface for AI mental-health support, where transcripts may be used to monitor depression severity and flag sessions requiring timely human review. However, robust PHQ-8 prediction across session regimes remains challenging: fine-tuning-based methods can exploit richer supervision but may generalize poorly under data scarcity, while prompt-based LLM methods are data-efficient but usually treat each transcript holistically and provide limited support for longitudinal context. We study robust depression tracking from counseling transcripts across single-session and multi-session regimes. We introduce LongCounsel, a multi-session counseling dataset with session-level PHQ-8 supervision for evaluating repeated-session tracking under partial symptom disclosure and cross-session continuity. We further propose EmoTrack, a PHQ-8 prediction framework that combines LLM-extracted clinical signals with frozen turn-level semantic embeddings and trains symptom-specific predictors over the resulting transcript representation. When prior sessions are available, EmoTrack can further incorporate them through compact cross-session memory. Experiments on LongCounsel and DAIC-WOZ show that EmoTrack achieves a clear gain on the real single-session benchmark, including a 13.5% relative MAE reduction over the strongest DAIC-WOZ baseline, and remains competitive with the strongest longitudinal baseline on LongCounsel.

### [139] [One LR Doesn't Fit All: Heavy-Tail Guided Layerwise Learning Rates for LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22297)
*Di He,Songjun Tu,Keyu Wang,Lu Yin,Shiwei Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对Transformer各层结构差异，本文提出了“层级学习率（LLR）”方案，利用重尾自正则化理论动态分配学习率，在低调优成本下实现了大模型训练效率与性能的双重提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前深度学习中对Transformer所有层采用统一学习率的做法，忽略了Transformer架构内部的结构异质性（Structural Heterogeneity），这限制了大语言模型（LLM）的训练效率和最终性能。因此，作者旨在设计一种能针对各层特性自适应调整学习率的机制，以实现更均衡的训练。

Method: 基于重尾自正则化（HT-SR）理论，通过分析权重相关矩阵的经验谱密度（ESD）来量化各层的“重尾性”。具体策略是：对重尾性较弱的层分配较大的学习率以加速学习，对重尾性较强的层分配较小的学习率以保持稳定性。该方法可直接从统一学习率的基线方案中迁移超参数配置，具有极低的调优成本。

Result: 实验涵盖了多种架构（LLaMA至GPT-nano）、优化器（AdamW和Muon）及参数规模（60M-1B）。结果显示，LLR实现了最高1.5倍的训练加速，并将平均零样本（zero-shot）准确率从47.09%提升至49.02%，证明了其在收敛速度和泛化能力上的显著优势。

Conclusion: 本文提出的层级学习率（LLR）策略证明了针对Transformer架构异构性进行精细化超参数调节的有效性。通过利用HT-SR理论实现学习率的自适应分配，不仅解决了统一学习率带来的训练不平衡问题，还显著提升了训练效率和模型性能，为大模型的训练优化提供了一种高效且易于迁移的新范式。

Abstract: Learning rate configuration is a fundamental aspect of modern deep learning. The prevailing practice of applying a uniform learning rate across all layers overlooks the structural heterogeneity of Transformers, potentially limiting their effectiveness as the backbone of Large Language Models (LLMs). In this paper, we introduce Layerwise Learning Rate (LLR), an adaptive scheme that assigns distinct learning rates to individual Transformer layers. Our method is grounded in Heavy-Tailed Self-Regularization (HT-SR) theory, which characterizes the empirical spectral density (ESD) of weight correlation matrices to quantify heavy-tailedness. Layers with weaker heavy-tailedness are assigned larger learning rates to accelerate their training, while layers with stronger heavy-tailedness receive smaller learning rates. By tailoring learning rates in this manner, LLR promotes balanced training across layers, leading to faster convergence and improved generalization. Extensive experiments across architectures (from LLaMA to GPT-nano), optimizers (AdamW and Muon), and parameter scales (60M-1B) demonstrate that LLR achieves up to 1.5x training speedup and outperforms baselines, notably raising average zero-shot accuracy from 47.09% to 49.02%. A key advantage of LLR is its low tuning overhead: it transfers nearly optimal LR settings directly from the uniform baseline. Code is available at https://github.com/hed-ucas/Layer-wise-Learning-Rate.

</details>


### [140] [SepsisAI Orchestrator: A Containerized and Scalable Platform for Deploying AI Models and Real-Time Monitoring in Early Sepsis Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22331)
*Santiago Ospitia,John Sanabria,John Garcia-Henao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文介绍了SepsisAI-Orchestrator平台，这是一个旨在解决临床AI模型部署难题的模块化基础设施。研究通过负载测试发现，模型推理的性能表现受容器副本配置影响呈现“U型”曲线，即副本数需与物理CPU线程数精准匹配才能实现最佳性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 临床机器学习模型在研究中表现优异，但受限于医疗环境中的系统级障碍（数据异构、缺乏标准化部署工作流、模型延迟要求高等），导致难以转化为实际临床应用。本文旨在构建一套标准化、可扩展的部署基础设施，以弥合临床AI研究与落地之间的鸿沟。

Method: 提出了SepsisAI-Orchestrator平台，采用模块化设计，结合HL7 FHIR架构进行数据预处理、NoSQL存储、容器化LightGBM分类器（通过REST API调用）以及Streamlit临床可视化仪表盘，并使用Docker与Kubernetes进行编排。利用k6负载测试工具在50-1000并发用户场景下评估系统性能。

Result: 研究发现，容器副本数与主机物理CPU线程数匹配时性能最优。在12线程CPU上，将副本数从3增加到12，p95延迟从3.3秒降至1.41秒（降低57.3%），并消除了请求失败；过度配置（24或48个副本）会因调度器竞争导致性能退化。

Conclusion: 本文通过实证研究揭示了临床AI推理工作负载中存在的“U型”扩展行为，强调了基础设施优化对于模型成功从实验室走向临床应用的重要性。合理的资源配置（如容器副本数与物理CPU线程数匹配）是平衡延迟与吞吐量的关键。

Abstract: Despite strong predictive results in the clinical machine learning literature, the translation of these models into bedside use remains limited by systems-level barriers: heterogeneous data representations, the absence of standardized deployment workflows, and a mismatch between research prototypes and the concurrency and latency requirements of hospital environments. We present the SepsisAI-Orchestrator, an open-source modular platform that addresses this deployment gap for early sepsis detection. The platform integrates HL7 FHIR-inspired Clinical Document Architecture (CDA) preprocessing, NoSQL storage, a containerized LightGBM classifier served via REST APIs, and a Streamlit clinical dashboard, orchestrated with Docker and Kubernetes. A previously validated LightGBM model (F1 0.87-0.94 on PhysioNet 2019) is reused without modification; the contribution lies in the surrounding infrastructure and its empirical characterization under load. Using k6 with 50-1000 concurrent virtual users, we find that replica count must be matched to the physical CPU thread count of the host: scaling from 3 to 12 replicas on a 12-thread CPU reduces p95 latency from 3.3s to 1.41s (57.3% reduction) and eliminates all request failures, while over-provisioning to 24 or 48 replicas degrades performance due to scheduler contention. To our knowledge this U-shaped scaling behavior has not been quantified previously for clinical AI inference workloads. We do not claim prospective clinical validation. Source code and deployment manifests are available at https://github.com/nucleusai/sepsisai-orchestrator.

### [141] [Learning Causal Orderings for In-Context Tabular Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22335)
*Sascha Xu,Sarah Mameche,Jilles Vreeken*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TabOrder是一种新型表格预测模型，它通过端到端学习并强制执行变量的因果拓扑排序，解决了传统基于相关性学习模型在分布偏移下的不稳定性，实现了因果结构发现与高效预测的有机结合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管上下文学习（In-context learning）在表格数据预测中表现优异，但其主要依赖相关性，在面对分布偏移或干预时表现不稳定。现有的因果发现方法虽然能识别结构，但往往与预测架构脱节。因此，本文旨在研究如何将因果拓扑排序直接融入预测模型，以提高模型的因果稳健性和预测效果。

Method: 提出了TabOrder模型，核心机制是“因果序约束注意力（causal order-constrained attention）”。该模型在非监督学习框架下，通过基于似然的目标函数自动学习变量的最优因果拓扑排序，并在预测过程中强制执行该排序，即仅允许目标变量依赖于因果序中排在其之前的特征。同时，文中还分析了缺失数据对因果方向识别的影响。

Result: 实验结果表明，TabOrder能够有效地恢复准确的变量因果排序。在预测任务和缺失值补全任务中，TabOrder均表现出优异的性能，并且在处理受干预的真实生物学数据时，展现了良好的解释能力。

Conclusion: TabOrder通过将因果排序集成到注意力机制中，成功弥合了因果发现与预测建模之间的鸿沟。该研究证明了在表格数据预测中引入因果拓扑约束不仅能提升模型的稳健性（特别是在面对分布偏移或干预时），还能同时完成预测和数据补全任务，为理解复杂数据（如生物学数据）提供了因果解释性。

Abstract: In-context learning for tabular data sets strong predictive standards in observational settings; it however primarily relies on correlational structure, which becomes unreliable under distribution shift or intervention. While established methods to discover causal structure exist, they are often focused on structure identifiability and decoupled from the predictive architectures that could benefit from them.
  To bridge these perspectives, we study how to simultaneously infer and enforce causal structure in the form of topological variable orderings into tabular prediction. Unlike standard architectures, our model TabOrder uses causal order-constrained attention, basing predictions only on features that precede a target under a learned causal order. Similar to causal discovery methods, TabOrder learns the optimal variable ordering in an unsupervised manner through a likelihood-based objective. We justify this choice under standard functional model classes and also study how sample missingness, a common challenge in tabular data, interacts with causal direction identification. Empirically, we confirm that TabOrder recovers accurate variable orderings while addressing prediction and imputation tasks, as well as gives insight into real-world biological data under intervention.

### [142] [Physics-Informed Generative Solver: Bridging Data-Driven Priors and Conservation Laws for Stable Spatiotemporal Field Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22338)
*Ziyuan Zhu,Keyu Hu,Zhifei Chen,Yuhao Shi,Ming Bao,Jing Zhao,Gang Wang,Haitan Xu,Jiadong Li,Qijun Zhao,Xiaodong Li,Minghui Lu,Yanfeng Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种物理信息生成求解器，通过结合稳定的得分匹配先验与推理时的物理残差引导，实现了从稀疏测量中精确重构遵循物理定律的连续场。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的数据驱动生成模型在从稀疏测量重构连续物理场时，往往会产生违反物理守恒定律的结果，且难以直接将第一性原理约束整合到生成过程中。

Method: 提出了一种物理信息生成求解器（Physics-informed generative solver），包含两个核心部分：1. 鞅正则化得分匹配（Martingale-Regularized Score Matching），通过得分福克-普朗克约束正则化先验学习，确保动力学稳定性；2. 物理信息隐式得分采样（Physics-Informed Implicit Score Sampling），在推理阶段利用物理残差的梯度引导去噪轨迹，将采样结果投影到物理可行的流形上，无需重新训练模型。

Result: 该方法在声学领域实现了压力与粒子速度的协同生成，构建了能抑制空间混叠的高密度虚拟阵列；同时在极度稀疏的ERA5气象场数据中表现出良好的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 该研究成功提出了一种将深度生成模型与物理定律结合的通用框架，能够有效解决高维反问题，为人工智能在物理科学领域的应用提供了严谨且具普适性的范式。

Abstract: Reconstructing continuous physical fields from sparse measurements is a central inverse problem, but data-driven generative models can produce states that violate governing dynamics. We introduce a physics-informed generative solver that separates stable prior learning from inference-time enforcement of conservation laws. Martingale-Regularized Score Matching regularizes score pretraining with a Score Fokker-Planck constraint, yielding a dynamically stable prior. Physics-Informed Implicit Score Sampling then guides denoising trajectories by gradients of physical residuals, projecting samples toward admissible manifolds without retraining. In acoustics, the method co-generates pressure and particle velocity from sparse sensors, enabling dense virtual arrays that suppress spatial aliasing. The same framework generalizes to real-world ERA5 meteorological fields under extreme sparsity. Together, this work establishes a rigorous and generalizable paradigm for solving high-dimensional inverse problems, bridging the gap between generative artificial intelligence and first-principles science.

### [143] [From Snapshots to Trajectories: Learning Single-Cell Gene Expression Dynamics via Conditional Flow Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22340)
*Siyu Pu,Qingqing Long,Xiaohan Huang,Haotian Chen,Jiajia Wang,Meng Xiao,Xiao Luo,Hengshu Zhu,Yuanchun Zhou,Xuezhi Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对单细胞测序数据中缺乏连续时间点的问题，该论文提出scFM模型，通过融合最优传输与双向流匹配技术，显著提升了细胞状态演化轨迹推断的准确性和长期预测的稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的单细胞RNA测序轨迹推断方法在处理非配对的时间快照数据时，面临局部转移模糊和长程预测中累积误差导致的分布漂移问题，迫切需要一种更稳定的动态建模方法。

Method: 提出了一种基于条件流匹配的潜在生成框架scFM：1. 利用熵正则化最优传输（OT）耦合构建软加权目标以学习时间相关速度场；2. 学习双向速度场以增强时间一致性并优化耦合；3. 引入分布级对齐和潜在动态正则化以校正长程预测中的分布漂移。

Result: 在真实单细胞时间序列数据集上的实验表明，scFM在时间插值和外推任务中均能持续提升分布预测性能，并能更准确地重构轨迹及恢复潜在的基因表达动态。

Conclusion: scFM通过结合最优传输和流匹配技术，有效解决了单细胞RNA测序数据中时间点离散、分布漂移及轨迹推断不准确的问题，实现了更精确的细胞动态建模。

Abstract: Single-cell RNA sequencing (scRNA-seq) provides high-dimensional profiles of cellular states, enabling data-driven modeling of cellular dynamics over time. In practice, time-resolved scRNA-seq is collected at only a few discrete time points as unpaired snapshot populations, leaving substantial temporal gaps. This motivates trajectory inference at unmeasured time points. Existing methods mainly follow two directions, optimal-transport (OT) alignment provides distribution-level matching between observed snapshots, while continuous-time generative models support forecasting via learned dynamics. However, two challenges remain: (i) unpaired snapshots render local transitions between adjacent time points ambiguous, leading to unstable supervision; and (ii) long-horizon prediction relies on repeated integration, where small modeling errors compound and cause distribution drift. To address these challenges, we propose single-cell Flow Matching (scFM), a latent generative framework based on coupling-conditioned flow matching. First, we compute entropically regularized OT couplings between adjacent snapshots and use them to construct soft, weighted flow-matching targets for learning time-dependent velocity fields. Second, we learn bidirectional velocity fields and leverage their consistency to refine couplings and improve temporal coherence under sparse supervision. Third, we introduce distribution-level alignment and latent dynamic regularization to anchor long rollouts and mitigate drift. Experiments on real-world time-series scRNA-seq datasets show that scFM consistently improves distributional prediction performance for both temporal interpolation and extrapolation. Moreover, scFM yields more accurate trajectory reconstruction and temporally coherent visualizations where intermediate time points are absent, indicating a more faithful recovery of underlying temporal gene expression dynamics.

### [144] [VeriScale: Adversarial Test-Suite Scaling for Verifiable Code Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22368)
*Yifan Bai,Xiaoyang Liu,Zihao Mou,Guihong Wang,Jian Yu,Shuhan Xie,Yantao Li,Yangyu Zhang,Jingwei Liang,Tao Luo*

TL;DR: 针对现有 LLM 代码基准测试评估不准确的问题，论文提出了 VeriScale 框架。该框架通过对抗性构造和精简测试用例，成功暴露了模型在代码生成任务中的隐蔽缺陷，并实现了评估准确性与计算效率的平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大语言模型（LLM）代码生成基准测试由于测试用例数量不足及质量受限，往往导致模型在功能正确性和形式化验证能力上被过高估计。该研究旨在通过构建更具挑战性的基准测试来准确衡量 LLM 的实际编程与验证能力。

Method: 提出了一个两阶段的评估框架 VeriScale：1. 测试套件扩展（Test-suite expansion）：利用对抗性实现构造多样化且具有挑战性的测试用例；2. 测试套件精简（Test-suite reduction）：将扩展后的测试集提炼为既紧凑又具高度辨别力的精简套件。作者基于此框架构建了 VerinaPlus 和 VerinaLite 数据集。

Result: VerinaPlus 将原始测试套件规模扩大了 83 倍，在八个主流 LLM 上的测试结果显示，模型在代码生成（CodeGen）和规范生成（SpecGen）任务上的得分均出现大幅下降，揭示了原先被掩盖的模型缺陷。VerinaLite 在仅保留 14 倍规模的情况下，仍保持了与 VerinaPlus 相近的评估辨别力，且大幅降低了评估成本。

Conclusion: VeriScale 框架通过对抗性实现有效解决了现有代码基准测试中测试用例不足的问题。实验表明，更全面且具有辨别力的测试套件能更真实地揭示大语言模型在代码生成和规范生成任务中的局限性，同时 VerinaLite 证明了在保持评估有效性的前提下显著降低计算成本的可行性。

Abstract: As large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed for software engineering, constructing high-quality benchmarks is crucial for evaluating not just the functional correctness, but also the formal verifiability of generated code. However, existing benchmarks are limited by the quantity and quality of positive and negative test cases, leading to an overestimation of model capabilities in generating specifications and implementations. To address this, we propose VeriScale, a novel framework driven by the adversarial implementations. It consists of two stages: test-suite expansion to construct diverse and challenging test cases, and test-suite reduction to distill them into compact yet discriminative suites. While VeriScale is general, we instantiate it on Verina to construct VerinaPlus, which expands the original test suites by over 83$\times$, and VerinaLite, a lightweight 14$\times$ variant. Our experiments across eight state-of-the-art LLMs demonstrate that VerinaPlus exposes substantial model weaknesses hidden by the original benchmark, evidenced by sharp score drops on both SpecGen and CodeGen tasks, whereas VerinaLite maintains this discriminative power at a fraction of the evaluation cost. The enhanced benchmarks and source code are publicly available at https://github.com/XiaoyangLiu-sjtu/VeriScale.

</details>


### [145] [ASAP: Attention Sink Anchored Pruning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22372)
*Jaehyuk Lee,Hanyoung Kim,Yanggee Kim,Donghun Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为ASAP的无需训练的ViT剪枝框架，通过将“注意力汇聚”转化为信息扩散分析工具，有效压缩了冗余Token，在显著提升ViT处理高分辨率任务的效率的同时，保持了优秀的模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ViT在高分辨率下的自注意力机制具有二次计算复杂度，而现有的令牌压缩方法多依赖单一层的注意力分数，容易受“注意力汇聚”（attention sink）现象干扰，导致非关键信息被错误保留，从而降低了模型推理效率。

Method: 本文提出了ASAP（注意力汇聚锚定剪枝）框架：1. 将ViT的信息流建模为“懒随机游走”（Lazy Random Walk）；2. 利用注意力汇聚点作为概率质量的累积中心；3. 计算向汇聚点的扩散距离；4. 通过径向扩散聚类划分Token，并采用转移权重池化压缩背景冗余。整个过程无需额外训练（Training-free）。

Result: ASAP在图像、视频及视觉-语言任务中均优于现有的前沿方法，在保持或提升模型精度的前提下，成功将推理吞吐量提升了高达48%。

Conclusion: ASAP通过将“注意力汇聚”（attention sink）视为信息流的核心特征，提供了一种无需训练、高效且鲁棒的ViT剪枝方案，证明了利用图论视角处理模型冗余的有效性，为高分辨率视觉任务的实时推理提供了有力支持。

Abstract: Vision Transformers (ViTs) face severe computational bottlenecks due to the quadratic complexity of self-attention at high resolutions. Existing token reduction methods rely on local metrics - such as single-layer attention scores - that are inherently vulnerable to the attention sink phenomenon, where uninformative tokens are paradoxically preserved over salient foreground objects. We propose ASAP (Attention Sink Anchored Pruning), a training-free framework that recasts this sink as a feature. Modeling ViT information flow as a Lazy Random Walk, ASAP identifies the sink as a dominant accumulator of probability mass. By computing the diffusion distance to the sink within the cumulative transition matrix, ASAP partitions tokens via Radial Diffusion Clustering and compresses background redundancy through Transition Weight Pooling in a single shot. Extensive experiments across image, video, and vision-language tasks demonstrate ASAP outperforms state-of-the-art methods, accelerating throughput by up to 48% while maintaining - or even exceeding - baseline accuracy.

### [146] [Target-Aligned Bellman Backup for Cross-domain Offline Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22376)
*Wei Liu,Ting Long*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对跨域离线强化学习中数据迁移可靠性问题，提出TABB方法，通过将数据选择的衡量标准从“局部转移相似性”转向“Bellman目标一致性”，有效提升了策略在目标域中的学习效率与表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的跨域离线强化学习方法多基于转移层面的相似性来评估源域数据的可用性，但这种方法忽略了长期回报的一致性，视觉或动态相似的转移可能在目标域中导致完全不同的结果，从而误导策略学习。

Method: 提出了一种名为“目标对齐Bellman备份”（Target-Aligned Bellman Backup, TABB）的方法。该方法摒弃了传统的基于转移特征相似性的度量，转而通过衡量源域数据对目标域Bellman目标估计的贡献度，来实现源域数据的选择性利用。

Result: 在多种跨域离线强化学习场景（特别是目标域数据极其匮乏的情况下）的实验中，TABB方法展现出了卓越的性能，显著优于现有的基准方法。

Conclusion: 本文提出的TABB方法通过以Bellman目标为核心的对齐评估，有效解决了跨域离线强化学习中仅依赖状态转移相似性带来的偏差问题，为数据跨域迁移提供了更稳健的决策依据。

Abstract: Cross-domain offline reinforcement learning (CDRL) aims to improve policy learning in a target domain by leveraging data collected from a source domain. Existing works typically assess the transferability of source-domain data by measuring its similarity to target-domain transitions, and implicitly perform transition-level selection. Transitions that are considered similar are assigned higher weights or rewards, while dissimilar ones are down-weighted. However, transition-level similarity does not necessarily imply consistency in long-term returns. Even visually or dynamically similar transitions may lead to significantly different outcomes in the target domain, which can mislead policy learning and degrade performance. To address this issue, we revisit the fundamental objective of policy learning. Since policy optimization ultimately relies on Bellman targets to evaluate the quality of decisions, we propose to assess the transferability of source-domain transitions based on their alignment with target-domain Bellman targets, rather than superficial transition similarity. Based on this insight, we propose a method termed Target-Aligned Bellman Backup (TABB), which selectively leverages source-domain data by measuring their contribution to accurate Bellman target estimation in the target domain. We evaluate TABB across a broad range of cross-domain offline RL settings with highly limited target-domain data. Experimental results show that TABB consistently achieves strong performance.

### [147] [AMUSE: Anytime Muon with Stable Gradient Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22432)
*Jueun Kim,Baekrok Shin,Jihun Yun,Beomhan Baek,Minhak Song,Chulhee Yun*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管 Muon 在深度学习优化中表现出色，但其机制尚不明确，且在大曲率方向（山谷壁）容易产生剧烈震荡。研究旨在探索 Muon 的工作原理，并解决其导致的优化轨迹不稳定性问题，同时消除对传统学习率调度的依赖。

Method: 提出了 AMUSE（Anytime MUon with Stable gradient Evaluation）算法。该方法结合了 Muon 的矩阵正交化更新机制（加速训练进度）与无调度平均化技术（抑制震荡），通过动态调节插值系数，在训练初期侧重于快速适应，在后期侧重于通过平均化实现轨迹平滑。

Result: 实验表明，AMUSE 在视觉任务和大语言模型预训练中，在性能与迭代次数的帕累托前沿（Pareto frontier）上均优于 Schedule-Free AdamW 和 Muon，且支持“随时（Anytime）”停止训练。

Conclusion: AMUSE 证明了将 Muon 的高效优化几何与无调度（Schedule-Free）的稳定性相结合，可以在无需预设学习率调度的情况下，实现更快的收敛和更好的性能，为大模型训练提供了一种更稳健的优化策略。

Abstract: Modern deep learning commonly relies on AdamW with prescribed learning rate schedules, but recent works challenge both components: Schedule-Free optimization removes explicit schedules via iterate averaging, and Muon improves the update geometry by orthogonalizing momentum for matrix parameters. Despite Muon's strong empirical performance, its underlying mechanism remains partially understood. We study Muon through the river-valley loss landscape, where useful training progress occurs along a flat, low-curvature bulk subspace (the river), while high-curvature dominant directions form steep valley walls that induce oscillations. We empirically show that while Muon's orthogonalization accelerates river progress by increasing the bulk component, it also amplifies dominant-direction noise, causing oscillatory trajectories. Building on this, we propose Anytime MUon with Stable gradient Evaluation (AMUSE), which integrates Muon's rapid bulk progress with the stabilizing effect of Schedule-Free averaging. AMUSE uses a time-varying interpolation coefficient that initially evaluates gradients near the fast Muon sequence for rapid adaptation, then gradually shifts toward the stable averaged sequence to suppress valley-wall oscillations. As a result, AMUSE requires no learning rate schedules and supports anytime training. Across vision tasks and large language model pretraining, AMUSE consistently improves the performance-iteration Pareto frontier over (Schedule-Free) AdamW and Muon.

### [148] [Understanding Multimodal Failure in Action-Chunking Behavioral Cloning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22493)
*Lorenzo Mazza,Massimiliano Datres,Ariel Rodriguez,Sebastian Bodenstedt,Gitta Kutyniok,Stefanie Speidel*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了行为克隆中“一对多”动作映射的挑战，指出潜变量模型与生成式模型在处理多模态分布时各有其内在的理论局限和失效机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 行为克隆在处理“一对多”映射（即相同观测对应多种有效动作）的任务时面临巨大挑战。现有方法在面对多模态分布时往往表现不佳，研究者旨在揭示不同模型参数化方式导致失效的深层原因。

Method: 作者深入剖析了两种主流的多模态行为克隆策略：潜变量策略（通过后验-先验正则化处理多模态）和动作空间生成式策略（利用基础空间到动作空间的映射）。通过理论推导和在合成任务及机器人模拟基准测试上的实验，分析了它们在处理多模态分布时的失效模式及制约因素。

Result: 实验表明，潜变量策略中过度的正则化会损失识别演示模态所需的动作条件信息，而弱正则化则依赖于先验分布对潜在空间的覆盖能力；生成式策略的性能受限于映射的Lipschitz常数，若要覆盖多个分离模态，往往导致平滑性丧失或产生无效的过渡区域。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了多模态行为克隆中存在的内在权衡：潜变量模型需要在正则化强度与保留模态信息之间取得平衡；生成式模型则受到Lipschitz连续性的制约。理解这些机制对于设计更可靠的机器人策略至关重要。

Abstract: Behavioral cloning becomes difficult when the same observation admits several valid actions. We study this problem for action-chunking policies and show that different multimodal parameterizations fail in different ways. For latent-variable policies, posterior-prior regularization makes deployment-time sampling more reliable, but excessive regularization removes the action-conditioned information needed to distinguish demonstrated modes. Reducing this regularization can preserve mode information, but then success depends on whether the prior covers the relevant latent regions. For action-space generative policies, multimodality is constrained by the smoothness of the base-to-action transport: a map with small Lipschitz constant cannot assign substantial probability to many well-separated modes. Covering many modes therefore requires either sharp transitions in base space or off-support bridge regions in action space. Experiments on synthetic multimodal tasks and robotic simulation benchmarks support these mechanisms.

### [149] [Lost in Tokenization: Fundamental Trade-offs in Graph Tokenization for Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22471)
*Maya Bechler-Speicher,Gilad Yehudai,Gil Harari,Clayton Sanford,Amir Globerson,Joan Bruna*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了图Transformer中“图到Token映射”（Tokenization）对模型表达能力的关键决定性作用，证明了不同Token化方案会导致模型在处理不同图任务时产生巨大的效率和精度差异，并建议通过融合互补的Token化策略来优化模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管Transformer在图学习领域应用广泛，但目前缺乏对其核心组件“Token化方案”如何影响模型表达能力和计算效率的系统性理论研究。作者旨在探究不同的图到Token映射方式如何决定图结构信息的获取，以及其对Transformer深度和任务适应性的具体影响。

Method: 本文从理论和实验两方面展开研究：在理论上，通过数学证明分析了谱（Spectral）、随机游走（Random-walk）和邻接（Adjacency）三种基础Token化方案的表达能力、信息损耗及转换难度，并推导了相应的计算深度下界；在实验上，通过受控的合成任务和真实世界数据集，验证了不同Tokenization方案在不同任务类型下的表现差异。

Result: 研究发现：1. 随机游走Token化存在不可逆的信息损耗；2. 谱Token化虽无信息损耗但对局部任务表现不佳（病态）；3. 存在计算深度下界，证明了特定Tokenization方案限制了模型对高效结构表示的恢复能力；4. 实验表明不同任务对结构信息有不同偏好，组合使用互补的Tokenization可显著增强Transformer的能力。

Conclusion: 图Transformer的表达能力在根本上受限于其所采用的“图到Token”映射方式（Tokenization）。不同的Token化方案会产生不同的计算深度需求，且无法通过有限深度的Transformer在不同映射方案间有效转换。研究强调了选择合适的结构化表示对于图学习任务的重要性，并建议通过组合互补的Tokenization策略来提升模型性能。

Abstract: Transformers have become a central architecture for graph learning, but their application to graphs requires first choosing a tokenization: a graph-to-token map that determines which structural information is exposed at the input. In this work, we show that this choice is a fundamental component of transformer expressivity. We examine three tokenizations that serve as building blocks for many existing graph tokenizations: spectral, random-walk, and adjacency tokenizations. We prove that different tokenizations induce distinct depth regimes: the same graph computation may be realizable by a shallow transformer under one tokenization, while requiring substantially larger depth under another. For example, we prove that random-walk tokenization is lossy for any walk length, making it impossible in general to recover the graph from it, and that while spectral tokenization is lossless, it is ill-conditioned for local tasks. We further show that although both random-walk and spectral tokenizations are derived from adjacency information, it is impossible for a limited-depth transformer to convert between tokenization families in general. In particular, we establish lower bounds and impossibility results showing that unfavorable tokenizations may preclude the efficient recovery of more suitable structural representations. Finally, we complement our theory with controlled experiments on synthetic and real-world tasks, validating the predicted separations and showing that different tasks favor different structural views, and combining complementary tokenizations allows the transformer to leverage distinct signals from each representation.

### [150] [Represented Is Not Computed: A Causal Test of Candidate Algorithmic Intermediates in a Transformer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22488)
*Ishita Darade,Sushrut Thorat*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过算术任务研究发现，Transformer模型虽然能通过线性探针提取出符合算法逻辑的中间状态，但这些状态并未真正驱动模型的最终输出。这一研究强调了仅凭探针技术来解释模型内部算法机制的局限性，并强调了因果分析的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的模型可解释性研究常依赖线性探针来推断模型内部的算法逻辑，但探针观察到的“表征”是否真正参与了因果决策过程尚不明确。该研究旨在通过一个定义明确的算术任务，通过对比“基于探针的可解释性分析”与“因果干预分析”，揭示这两者之间可能存在的矛盾。

Method: 1. 任务设计：训练Transformer执行“基数提取”任务（计算$N$在$B$进制下第$D$位的数值）；2. 探针技术：使用线性探针（Linear Probes）检测模型是否表征了算法所需的中间变量（如$N/B^D$）；3. 因果分析：采用因果介入测试（Causal Tests）验证特定表征在输出生成中的实际作用；4. 电路搜索：利用稀疏电路搜索（Sparse Circuit Search）定位并分析信息流动的路径。

Result: 1. 模型在基数提取任务上达到99.83%的准确率；2. 探针实验显示模型内部存在与封闭解一致的中间变量表征；3. 因果分析和电路搜索发现，模型实际上采用了与 probe 指示的“分步计算”不同的策略，中间变量并未通过探测到的路径传导至输出层，证明了“可解码性”并不等同于“因果作用”。

Conclusion: 研究表明，基于线性探针得出的中间表征结论可能与模型实际的因果机制存在显著偏差。尽管模型内部确实表征了符合算法逻辑的中间变量，但这些变量并非直接驱动输出的因果路径。这一发现警示研究者在使用探针解释深度模型内部机理时应持谨慎态度，必须通过因果介入实验进行验证。

Abstract: Structured prompts require integrating components according to task-relevant relations. How a network implements this integration is often hard to judge in language or vision, where those relations are rarely specified precisely enough to define a candidate internal algorithm. Arithmetic offers a cleaner setting. We study a Transformer trained on base-digit extraction: given $N$, $B$, and $D$, it must report the coefficient of $B^D$ in the base-$B$ expansion of $N$. The closed-form solution, $\lfloor N/B^D \rfloor \bmod B$, provides explicit candidate algorithmic intermediates. Across three seeds, the model reaches 99.83% exact-answer accuracy on held-out number-base intersections, establishing reliable task competence. Linear probes decode the intermediates, making staged arithmetic computation plausible. Causal tests then separate representation from use: within the localized route from the stream with $D$ as input to the output positions, behavior depends on early $D$-selective communication, independent of $N$ and $B$. Relatedly, a sparse circuit search finds mostly separate $N$, $B$, and $D$ routes that combine late rather than the staged route suggested by the probes. Thus, the model represents the intermediates that make the closed-form solution plausible, but the identified localized causal route does not transmit them to the output stream. This case shows that probe-based conclusions can diverge sharply from causal observations, even when explicit algorithmic hypotheses are available.

</details>


### [151] [The Signal in the Noise: OOD Detection Through Goodness-of-Fit Testing in Factorised Latent Spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22496)
*Philipp Bomatter,Jack Geary,Henry Gouk*

TL;DR: 针对生成模型似然估计在OOD检测中的失效问题，本文提出了SITN方法，通过分析数据在归一化流潜在空间中的非典型噪声特征，实现了高效且鲁棒的单样本OOD检测。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种名为“信号在噪声中”（Signal in the Noise, SITN）的新方法。该方法利用连续归一化流（Continuous Normalising Flows）的微分同胚和保质特性，观察到OOD样本在映射到潜在空间（噪声空间）后呈现出与训练数据显著不同的分布特征，并据此设计检测策略。

Conclusion: 本文提出的SITN方法利用连续归一化流的特性，成功解决了生成模型在OOD检测中由于似然估计不可靠而导致的性能问题，证明了通过分析噪声空间中的分布特性，可以实现高效且无复杂性偏差的异常检测。

Abstract: Deep generative models offer a natural foundation for out-of-distribution (OOD) detection, yet prior work has shown that their assigned likelihoods are notoriously unreliable indicators for in- vs out-of-distribution data. In this paper, we address this problem by leveraging the diffeomorphic and mass-preserving properties of continuous normalising flows. Our analysis shows that OOD samples are mapped to noise samples that are highly atypical under the noise prior in ways not captured by the likelihood. Based on this observation, we propose a new method -- Signal in the Noise (SITN) -- for OOD detection on the single-sample level. SITN requires no access to OOD data, incurs minimal computational overhead, and provides strict control of false positive rates. Comprehensive evaluations through standard benchmarks and synthetic perturbations highlight the method's effectiveness and the absence of the complexity bias inherent to likelihood-based methods.

</details>


### [152] [The Value of Covariance Matching in Gaussian DDPMs and the Lanczos Sampler](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22723)
*Md Sahil Akhtar,Aymane El Gadarri,Vivek F. Farias,Adam D. Jozefiak*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文解决了DDPM中因反向协方差假设导致的路径KL误差问题，提出了一种利用Lanczos迭代进行高效全协方差匹配的采样方法（LGS），在提升图像采样质量的同时避免了大规模矩阵运算，实现了理论与实践的双重优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的高斯DDPM标准各向同性反向协方差在去噪步数 $T$ 增加时，存在无法避免的 $Ω(1/T)$ 路径KL散度误差。这种误差在需要对完整逆向轨迹进行扰动（如分类器引导）的场景中表现尤为严重，因此需要寻找一种更优的协方差匹配策略以减少误差。

Method: 1. 提出通过匹配完整的后验协方差来打破标准各向同性协方差在路径KL误差上 $Ω(1/T)$ 的下界；
2. 引入“Lanczos高斯采样器（LGS）”：一种无需训练、无需存储密集矩阵的采样方法，仅利用协方差-向量乘积（通过雅可比-向量乘积实现）；
3. 证明了LGS的近似误差随Lanczos迭代次数呈指数级衰减。

Result: 1. 理论上证明了全协方差匹配可将路径KL误差降低至 $O(1/T^2)$；
2. LGS方法在只需极少（如3次）Lanczos迭代的情况下，即可在多个图像基准测试中超越现有的强基线模型（如OCM-DDPM），显著提升了采样质量。

Conclusion: 研究证明了通过匹配全协方差可以显著降低去噪扩散概率模型（DDPM）在路径空间中的KL散度误差。提出的Lanczos高斯采样器（LGS）是一种高效、无需训练的近似方法，证明了在保持计算可行性的同时，可以实现理论上的性能提升，为快速且高质量的DDPM采样提供了新的范式。

Abstract: A central error measure in Gaussian DDPMs is the path-space KL divergence between the exact reverse chain and the learned Gaussian reverse process. This quantity is especially relevant for procedures such as classifier guidance, which perturb the entire reverse trajectory rather than only the terminal sample. Prior analyses show that standard isotropic reverse covariances suffer an unavoidable $Ω(1/T)$ path-KL error as the number of denoising steps $T$ grows. We show that matching the full posterior covariance breaks this barrier, yielding an order-wise improvement that reduces the path KL to $O(1/T^2)$. To make full covariance matching practical, we introduce the Lanczos Gaussian sampler (LGS), a training-free, matrix-free method for sampling from the optimal reverse covariance using only covariance-vector products, which are available through Jacobian-vector products of the posterior mean. LGS avoids dense covariance storage and auxiliary covariance models. We prove that LGS approximation error decays exponentially in the number of Lanczos steps, where each Lanczos step requires a single Jacobian-vector product. Empirically, using only just three such steps improves sample quality over strong diagonal-covariance baselines, including OCM-DDPM, across standard image benchmarks. This identifies full covariance matching as both theoretically valuable and practically accessible for fast DDPM sampling.

</details>


### [153] [Generative Modeling by Value-Driven Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22507)
*Pablo Moreno-Muñoz,Adrian Müller,Gergely Neu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为“值驱动传输”（VDT）的生成建模框架，通过随机控制理论将生成过程建模为线性规划问题。VDT能够实现比传统扩散模型更平直的采样路径，在保持模型高度灵活性的同时，显著提升了生成效率和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于流、扩散模型或薛定谔桥的生成模型在采样路径曲率、计算复杂度和效率方面仍存在局限性。本文旨在通过随机控制理论，寻找一种能够实现更直、更高效的传输路径，并兼具现有生成模型灵活性与可扩展性的新型建模方法。

Method: 本文提出了一种基于测度传输离散时间随机控制的新型生成框架。其核心方法是将生成问题形式化为一个线性规划（LP），利用该问题的对偶变量（即最优值函数）来推导最优控制策略。研究者进一步开发了一种无需模拟的原始-对偶（primal-dual）算法，用于高效求解最优值函数，并据此构建了“值驱动传输”（Value-Driven Transport, VDT）策略。该方法支持条件生成、分类器引导及非配对数据转换等扩展功能。

Result: 实验结果表明，VDT模型能够生成更平直的传输路径，从而在采样速度和鲁棒性上优于现有的扩散模型和流模型。在多项生成任务中，VDT展现出了强大的性能表现，并证明了其良好的可扩展性，同时能够轻松集成条件生成与引导技术。

Conclusion: 本研究提出了一种基于离散时间随机控制的生成建模新框架，该框架通过线性规划对偶变量表征最优值函数，从而实现了高效的生成策略。VDT模型在保持与扩散模型同等灵活性的同时，提供了更平直的传输路径，显著提升了采样效率和鲁棒性。

Abstract: We propose a new framework for generative modeling based on a discrete-time stochastic control formulation of measure transport. Adapting classic results from control theory, we formulate our problem as a linear program whose dual variables correspond to the \emph{optimal value function} of the control problem, which directly encodes the optimal control policy. Exploiting this LP formulation, we develop an efficient simulation-free primal-dual algorithm for computing approximately optimal value functions and the associated \emph{value-driven transport} (VDT) policies which approximate the true optimal policy. We show that well-trained VDT policies enjoy numerous favorable properties in comparison with other state-of-the-art methods based on flows, diffusions, or Schrödinger bridges: they lead to straight transport paths which can be simulated quickly and robustly, and can be enhanced in all the same ways as diffusion and flow-based models (e.g., conditional generation, classifier-free guidance, unpaired data-to-data translation are all easy to incorporate). We evaluate our methodology in a range of experiments, with results that indicate strong performance and good potential for scalability.

</details>


### [154] [Disentanglement Beyond Generative Models with Riemannian ICA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22531)
*Edmond Cunningham*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为“黎曼ICA”（RICA）的新框架，利用黎曼几何和解耦张量，在不依赖全局生成假设的情况下，实现了对现代表示学习中局部解耦特征的理论建模与分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的解耦理论大多依赖于统计独立的全局生成模型假设，这与现代预训练编码器的实际应用场景存在显著脱节。现有模型难以在不假设全局生成机制的前提下，对复杂现代特征进行解释。作者旨在建立一种能够解释现代表示学习中特征解耦特性的局部几何理论。

Method: 提出了“黎曼独立成分分析”（RICA），通过引入黎曼几何，将ICA的全局生成模型替换为基于局部几何结构的分析。核心方法是利用“解耦张量”（disentanglement tensor），该张量结合了数据对数似然的Hessian矩阵和模型诱导的Ricci曲率，用于表征数据点的“点状解耦”（pointwise disentanglement）。

Result: 在已知地面真值源的受控恢复任务中，RICA在多种流形结构上均能有效恢复源信息。实验表明，RICA的性能表现优于传统的ICA基线，且其表现不依赖于观测数据的坐标表示，证明了其在局部解耦分析中的稳健性与理论优势。

Conclusion: 本文通过黎曼几何成功地将解耦理论从传统的全局生成模型扩展到了局部几何结构。黎曼ICA（RICA）提供了一个无需依赖强生成假设的理论框架，能够更准确地解释现代预训练编码器所习得的特征，为理解高维数据中的独立变分因素提供了更稳健的数学工具。

Abstract: There is a gap between the theoretical foundations of disentanglement and the practice of modern representation learning. Existing theoretical frameworks, particularly Independent Component Analysis (ICA) and its nonlinear variants, assume a generative model with statistically independent latent variables underlying the data so that disentanglement amounts to identifying the latents that could have generated the data. This generative framework is interpretable and theoretically justified, but its strong assumptions make it difficult to apply to modern representation learning. Modern pretrained encoders often learn features that exhibit disentangled properties without making generative assumptions, yet there is no general theory for interpreting these features as independent factors of variation. We take a step toward such a theory by introducing Riemannian ICA (RICA), which replaces ICA's global generative model with local geometric structure. RICA is founded on the observation that in ICA, the factors of variation underlying a data point can be understood through radial curves emanating from the point that map to axis-aligned lines in the latent space. We formalize this perspective using Riemannian geometry and introduce our theory in a way that is consistent with the existing generative approach. Our main contribution is the disentanglement tensor, which encodes a second-order notion of disentanglement that we call pointwise disentanglement. This tensor depends on the Hessian of the data log likelihood as well as the Ricci curvature induced by the model. In a controlled source recovery setting with known ground-truth sources, RICA recovers sources across several manifolds, while the success of ICA baselines depends on the coordinates used to represent the observations. Our work provides a theoretical basis for studying local disentanglement without assuming a global generative model.

</details>


### [155] [Relational Linear Properties in Language Models: An Empirical Investigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22532)
*Giovanni Valer,Luigi Gresele,Marco Bronzini,Emanuele Marconato*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于KL散度的高效探针方法，用于量化评估语言模型中的“关系线性”假设，验证了该属性随模型层级和查询表述变化的规律，并证实了其在解释模型内部表征结构方面的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型的表征中普遍存在线性属性，但实验性地量化和验证这些属性仍具挑战。本文旨在验证“关系线性”假设（即固定关系下，主体嵌入向量可通过线性映射预测目标解码向量），并分析该属性在不同层级及不同表述方式下的变化规律。

Method: 本文提出了一种基于库尔巴克-莱布勒散度（Kullback-Leibler divergence）的探针方法，用于量化和测试关系线性。该方法通过评估从主体向量到目标向量的线性映射预测能力，避开了传统方法中粗糙的雅可比矩阵近似，实现了更高效的实验验证。

Result: 通过四个数据集的实证分析，研究发现关系线性在模型中的表现并不均一，呈现出明显的层级差异。实验结果证实了该属性与模型捕捉语言信息的方式相关，并受查询语句表述变化的影响，同时也证明了所提评估方法的优越性与高效性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，关系线性不仅在不同语言模型间存在差异，且呈现出层级模式，这种模式与模型中语言信息的分布特征相吻合。此外，该属性对关系的表述方式敏感，研究提出了一种比以往方法更高效、更精确的评估手段，验证了关系线性假设在现代大语言模型中的表现。

Abstract: Linear properties are ubiquitous in the representations of language models; however, testing them experimentally remains a challenging task. This work focuses on relational linearity: the hypothesis that, for a fixed relation (e.g., "plays"), the unembedding of an object (e.g., "trumpet") can be predicted from the embedding of its subject (e.g.,"Miles Davis") by a linear map. We present an experimental method to test the formulation of relational linearity by Marconato et al. (2025). Specifically, we introduce a probing method, based on Kullback-Leibler divergence, to evaluate this property and examine its variation across layers and paraphrased relational queries. It is also more efficient than previous work; for example, it avoids the crude Jacobian approximations used in Linear Relational Embeddings by Hernandez et al. (2024). Our findings across four datasets show that relational linearity varies across models, exhibits layer-wise patterns consistent with prior observations about linguistic information in model representations, and is differently affected by changes in how the relation is phrased.
